1. Computing threshold functions using dendrites

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/1611.03321v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Neurons, modeled as linear threshold unit (LTU), can in theory compute all thresh- old functions. In practice, however, some of these functions require synaptic weights of arbitrary large precision. We show here that dendrites can alleviate this requirement. We introduce here the non-Linear Threshold Unit (nLTU) that integrates synaptic input sub-linearly within distinct subunits to take into account local saturation in dendrites. We systematically search parameter space of the nTLU and TLU to compare them. Firstly, this shows that the nLTU can compute all threshold functions with smaller precision weights than the LTU. Secondly, we show that a nLTU can compute significantly more functions than a LTU when an input can only make a single synapse. This work paves the way for a new generation of network made of nLTU with binary synapses.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

LTU需要高精度的权重才能计算所有阈值函数，而nLTU的权重精度要求相对较低，但仍能计算比LTU更多的阈值函数。nLTU特别适用于单突触输入的情况，这使得它在某些神经网络中具有优势。此外，dendrites的存在能够进一步缓解权重精度的要求，使得nLTU在实际应用中更加灵活。阈值函数的计算依赖于神经元模型的精确度，因此，nLTU在输入只能形成一个突触时的优势更加明显，这可能使其成为新一代具有二进制突触的网络的理想选择。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • LTU需要高精度的权重才能计算所有阈值函数。
  • nLTU的权重精度要求低于LTU。
  • nLTU能计算比LTU更多的阈值函数。
  • nLTU适用于单突触输入的情况。
  • nLTU可能用于新一代具有二进制突触的网络。
  • dendrites能缓解权重精度要求的问题。
  • 阈值函数的计算依赖于神经元模型的精确度。
  • 输入只能形成一个突触时，nLTU的优势更明显。

2. Path-conditioned training: a principled way to rescale ReLU neural networks

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.19799v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Despite recent algorithmic advances, we still lack principled ways to leverage the well-documented rescaling symmetries in ReLU neural network parameters. While two properly rescaled weights implement the same function, the training dynamics can be dramatically different. To offer a fresh perspective on exploiting this phenomenon, we build on the recent path-lifting framework, which provides a compact factorization of ReLU networks. We introduce a geometrically motivated criterion to rescale neural network parameters which minimization leads to a conditioning strategy that aligns a kernel in the path-lifting space with a chosen reference. We derive an efficient algorithm to perform this alignment. In the context of random network initialization, we analyze how the architecture and the initialization scale jointly impact the output of the proposed method. Numerical experiments illustrate its potential to speed up training.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

rescaling symmetries在ReLU神经网络参数中被广泛记录，但缺乏利用这些对称性的原则方法。首先，两个适当缩放的权重可以实现相同的函数，但训练动力学可能截然不同。其次，path-lifting框架提供了一种紧凑的ReLU网络分解，有助于理解权重缩放的影响。此外，基于几何动机的准则用于最小化神经网络参数的缩放，这导致一种条件策略，将路径提升空间中的核与选定参考对齐。分析了架构和初始化缩放如何共同影响所提出方法的输出，数值实验表明，该方法有潜力加速训练。因此，尽管有算法进展，仍缺乏利用ReLU神经网络参数中记录的缩放对称性的原则方法。路径条件训练提供了一种原则性的方法来重新缩放ReLU神经网络，以优化训练动态。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • rescaling symmetries在ReLU神经网络参数中被广泛记录，但缺乏利用这些对称性的原则方法。
  • 两个适当缩放的权重实现相同的函数，但训练动力学可能截然不同。
  • path-lifting框架提供了一种紧凑的ReLU网络分解，有助于理解权重缩放的影响。
  • 几何动机的准则用于最小化神经网络参数的缩放，这导致一种条件策略，将路径提升空间中的核与选定参考对齐。
  • 分析了架构和初始化缩放如何共同影响所提出方法的输出。
  • 数值实验表明，该方法有潜力加速训练。
  • 尽管有算法进展，仍缺乏利用ReLU神经网络参数中记录的缩放对称性的原则方法。
  • 路径条件训练提供了一种原则性的方法来重新缩放ReLU神经网络，以优化训练动态。

3. HyperParallel: A Supernode-Affinity AI Framework

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03731v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The emergence of large-scale, sparse, multimodal, and agentic AI models has coincided with a shift in hardware toward supernode architectures that integrate hundreds to thousands of accelerators with ultra-low-latency interconnects and unified memory pools. However, existing AI frameworks are not designed to exploit these architectures efficiently, leading to high programming complexity, load imbalance, and poor memory utilization. In this paper, we propose a supernode-affinity AI framework that treats the supernode as a single logical computer and embeds hardware-aware orchestration into the framework. Implemented in MindSpore, our HyperParallel architecture comprises HyperOffload for automated hierarchical memory management, HyperMPMD for fine-grained MPMD parallelism across heterogeneous workloads, and HyperShard for declarative parallel strategy specification. Together, these techniques significantly improve training and inference efficiency while reducing parallel programming and system tuning overhead, demonstrating the necessity of supernode affinity for next-generation AI frameworks.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

supernode架构集成了数百到数千个加速器，具有超低延迟的互连和统一的内存池，这使得它成为下一代高性能计算平台的理想选择。然而，现有AI框架并未设计用于高效利用这些架构，导致高编程复杂性、负载不平衡和糟糕的内存利用率。为了解决这些问题，HyperParallel框架将supernode视为单个逻辑计算机，并嵌入了硬件感知的编排，从而显著提高了训练和推理效率。此外，HyperOffload技术实现了自动分层内存管理，而HyperMPMD技术则实现了细粒度的跨异构工作负载的MPMD并行，进一步优化了性能。HyperShard技术则通过实现声明式的并行策略指定，进一步简化了并行编程和系统调优的开销。因此，supernode亲和性对于下一代AI框架是必要的，这些技术共同确保了高效利用supernode架构的潜力。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • supernode架构集成了数百到数千个加速器，具有超低延迟的互连和统一的内存池。
  • 现有AI框架未设计用于高效利用这些架构，导致高编程复杂性、负载不平衡和糟糕的内存利用率。
  • HyperParallel框架将supernode视为单个逻辑计算机，并嵌入了硬件感知的编排。
  • HyperOffload技术实现了自动分层内存管理。
  • HyperMPMD技术实现了细粒度的跨异构工作负载的MPMD并行。
  • HyperShard技术实现了声明式的并行策略指定。
  • 这些技术显著提高了训练和推理效率，同时减少了并行编程和系统调优的开销。
  • supernode亲和性对于下一代AI框架是必要的。

4. Few-Shot Classification with Feature Map Reconstruction Networks

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2012.01506v2
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In this paper we reformulate few-shot classification as a reconstruction problem in latent space. The ability of the network to reconstruct a query feature map from support features of a given class predicts membership of the query in that class. We introduce a novel mechanism for few-shot classification by regressing directly from support features to query features in closed form, without introducing any new modules or large-scale learnable parameters. The resulting Feature Map Reconstruction Networks are both more performant and computationally efficient than previous approaches. We demonstrate consistent and substantial accuracy gains on four fine-grained benchmarks with varying neural architectures. Our model is also competitive on the non-fine-grained mini-ImageNet and tiered-ImageNet benchmarks with minimal bells and whistles.

5. Improving performance of real-time full-band blind packet-loss concealment with predictive network

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2211.04071v6
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Packet loss concealment (PLC) is a tool for enhancing speech degradation caused by poor network conditions or underflow/overflow in audio processing pipelines. We propose a real-time recurrent method that leverages previous outputs to mitigate artefact of lost packets without the prior knowledge of loss mask. The proposed full-band recurrent network (FRN) model operates at 48 kHz, which is suitable for high-quality telecommunication applications. Experiment results highlight the superiority of FRN over an offline non-causal baseline and a top performer in a recent PLC challenge.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

PLC工具旨在通过改善由网络条件差或音频处理管道中的下溢/上溢引起的语音降级来提升语音质量。FRN模型无需依赖损失掩码即可利用先前输出来减轻丢失包的伪影，这使得它在处理语音包丢失时更为高效。此外，FRN模型在48 kHz下运行，特别适用于高质量的电信应用。实验结果表明，FRN模型在减轻语音包丢失的影响方面优于非因果的离线基线和最近PLC挑战中的顶级性能模型。因此，FRN方法不仅能够实时预测并减轻包丢失的影响，还无需依赖损失掩码的先验知识，从而提升了其在实际应用中的灵活性和可靠性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • PLC工具旨在改善由网络条件差或音频处理管道中的下溢/上溢引起的语音降级。
  • FRN模型无需先验丢失掩码即可利用先前输出来减轻丢失包的伪影。
  • FRN模型在48 kHz下运行，适用于高质量的电信应用。
  • 实验结果表明FRN优于非因果的离线基线和最近PLC挑战中的顶级性能模型。
  • FRN方法是实时的，能够预测并减轻包丢失的影响。
  • 损失掩码的先验知识对于FRN模型不是必需的。

6. Spiky Rank and Its Applications to Rigidity and Circuits

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23503v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We introduce spiky rank, a new matrix parameter that enhances blocky rank by combining the combinatorial structure of the latter with linear-algebraic flexibility. A spiky matrix is block-structured with diagonal blocks that are arbitrary rank-one matrices, and the spiky rank of a matrix is the minimum number of such matrices required to express it as a sum. This measure extends blocky rank to real matrices and is more robust for problems with both combinatorial and algebraic character. Our conceptual contribution is as follows: we propose spiky rank as a well-behaved candidate matrix complexity measure and demonstrate its potential through applications. We show that large spiky rank implies high matrix rigidity, and that spiky rank lower bounds yield lower bounds for depth-2 ReLU circuits, the basic building blocks of neural networks. On the technical side, we establish tight bounds for random matrices and develop a framework for explicit lower bounds, applying it to Hamming distance matrices and spectral expanders. Finally, we relate spiky rank to other matrix parameters, including blocky rank, sparsity, and the $γ_2$-norm.

7. IU: Imperceptible Universal Backdoor Attack

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.00711v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Backdoor attacks pose a critical threat to the security of deep neural networks, yet existing efforts on universal backdoors often rely on visually salient patterns, making them easier to detect and less practical at scale. In this work, we introduce a novel imperceptible universal backdoor attack that simultaneously controls all target classes with minimal poisoning while preserving stealth. Our key idea is to leverage graph convolutional networks (GCNs) to model inter-class relationships and generate class-specific perturbations that are both effective and visually invisible. The proposed framework optimizes a dual-objective loss that balances stealthiness (measured by perceptual similarity metrics such as PSNR) and attack success rate (ASR), enabling scalable, multi-target backdoor injection. Extensive experiments on ImageNet-1K with ResNet architectures demonstrate that our method achieves high ASR (up to 91.3%) under poisoning rates as low as 0.16%, while maintaining benign accuracy and evading state-of-the-art defenses. These results highlight the emerging risks of invisible universal backdoors and call for more robust detection and mitigation strategies.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，图卷积网络（GCNs）能够建模不同类之间的关系，使得生成的类特定扰动既有效又难以察觉。其次，所提出的框架通过优化双重目标损失函数，平衡了隐身性和攻击成功率。此外，这种不可感知的通用后门攻击能够在极低的污染率（如0.16%）下实现高攻击成功率，并且在后门注入的同时保持了正常的准确率。因此，最先进的防御手段被该方法所规避，这表明不可感知的通用后门攻击带来了新的风险，需要开发出有效的检测和缓解策略。此外，使用感知相似性度量指标（如PSNR）来衡量隐身性，表明该方法能够实现可扩展的、针对多个目标的后门注入。因此，不可感知的通用后门攻击不仅能够控制所有目标类，而且能够在极低的污染率下实现高攻击成功率，同时保持了正常的准确率，从而对现有的防御手段构成了挑战。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • graph convolutional networks (GCNs) can model inter-class relationships.
  • class-specific perturbations generated are both effective and visually invisible.
  • the proposed framework optimizes a dual-objective loss balancing stealthiness and attack success rate.
  • imperceptible universal backdoor attacks can control all target classes with minimal poisoning.
  • poisoning rates as low as 0.16% can achieve high attack success rates.
  • benign accuracy is maintained despite the backdoor injection.
  • state-of-the-art defenses are evaded by the proposed method.
  • invisible universal backdoors pose emerging risks that need robust detection and mitigation strategies.
  • perceptual similarity metrics such as PSNR measure stealthiness.
  • the proposed method enables scalable, multi-target backdoor injection.

8. Virtual-Memory Assisted Buffer Management In Tiered Memory

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03271v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Tiered memory architectures have gained significant traction in the database community in recent years. In these architectures, the on-chip DRAM of the host processor is typically referred to as local memory, and forms the primary tier. Additional byte-addressable, cache-coherent memory resources, collectively referred to as remote memory (RMem, for short), form one or more secondary tiers. RMem is slower than local DRAM but faster than disk, e.g., NUMA memory located on a remote socket, chiplet-attached memory, and memory attached via high-performance interconnect protocols, e.g., RDMA and CXL. In this paper, we discuss how traditional two-tier (DRAM-Disk) virtual-memory assisted Buffer Management techniques generalize to an $n$-tier setting (DRAM-RMem-Disk). We present vmcache$^n$, an $n$-tier virtual-memory-assisted buffer pool that leverages the virtual memory subsystem and operating system calls to migrate pages across memory tiers. In this setup, page migration can become a bottleneck. To address this limitation, we introduce the move_pages2 system call that provides vmcache$^n$ with fine-grained control over the page migration process. Experiments show that vmcache$^n$ can a
  • 易漏细节梳理：

$n$-tier设置下的虚拟内存辅助缓冲管理技术，特别是vmcache$^n$，可以显著提高查询吞吐量，但同时也可能成为性能瓶颈。这是因为远程内存（RMem）虽然比本地DRAM慢，但比磁盘快，因此在多层设置中，远程内存可能包括NUMA内存、芯片级内存和高速互连协议下的内存。此外，页迁移过程的细粒度控制可以通过`move_pages2`系统调用实现，但在多层设置中，页迁移可能成为瓶颈，导致整体性能下降。因此，尽管传统两层缓冲管理技术可以推广到多层设置，但在$n$-tier环境中，需要更加精细地管理页迁移，以避免成为性能瓶颈。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • $n$-tier设置下的虚拟内存辅助缓冲管理技术可能成为性能瓶颈。
  • 远程内存（RMem）比本地DRAM慢，但比磁盘快。
  • 页迁移过程的细粒度控制可以通过`move_pages2`系统调用实现。
  • vmcache$^n$可以显著提高查询吞吐量。
  • 传统两层缓冲管理技术可以推广到多层设置。
  • 远程内存可能包括NUMA内存、芯片级内存和高速互连协议下的内存。
  • 页迁移在多层设置中可能成为瓶颈。

[2603.03271v1] Virtual-Memory Assisted Buffer Management In Tiered Memory Computer Science > Databases arXiv:2603.03271v1 (cs) [Submitted on 3 Mar 2026] Title: Virtual-Memory Assisted Buffer Management In Tiered Memory Authors: Yeasir Rayhan , Walid G. Aref View a PDF of the paper titled Virtual-Memory Assisted Buffer Management In Tiered Memory, by Yeasir Rayhan and Walid G. Aref View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Tiered memory architectures have gained significant traction in the database community in recent years. In these architectures, the on-chip DRAM of the host processor is typically referred to as local memory, and forms the primary tier. Additional byte-addressable, cache-coherent memory resources, collectively referred to as remote memory (RMem, for short), form one or more secondary tiers. RMem is slower than local DRAM but faster than disk, e.g., NUMA memory located on a remote socket, chiplet-attached memory, and memory attached via high-performance interconnect protocols, e.g., RDMA and CXL. In this paper, we discuss how traditional two-tier (DRAM-Disk) virtual-memory assisted Buffer Management techniques generalize to an $n$-tier setting (DRAM-RMem-Disk). We present vmcache$^n$, an $n$-tier virtual-memory-assisted buffer pool that leverages the virtual memory subsystem and operating system calls to migrate pages across memory tiers. In this setup, page migration can become a bottleneck. To address this limitation, we introduce the move_pages2 system call that provides vmcache$^n$ with fine-grained control over the page migration process. Experiments show that vmcache$^n$ can achieve up to 4$\times$ higher query throughput over vmcache for TPC-C workloads. 9. Why Do Neural Networks Forget: A Study of Collapse in Continual Learning

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04580v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Catastrophic forgetting is a major problem in continual learning, and lots of approaches arise to reduce it. However, most of them are evaluated through task accuracy, which ignores the internal model structure. Recent research suggests that structural collapse leads to loss of plasticity, as evidenced by changes in effective rank (eRank). This indicates a link to forgetting, since the networks lose the ability to expand their feature space to learn new tasks, which forces the network to overwrite existing representations. Therefore, in this study, we investigate the correlation between forgetting and collapse through the measurement of both weight and activation eRank. To be more specific, we evaluated four architectures, including MLP, ConvGRU, ResNet-18, and Bi-ConvGRU, in the split MNIST and Split CIFAR-100 benchmarks. Those models are trained through the SGD, Learning-without-Forgetting (LwF), and Experience Replay (ER) strategies separately. The results demonstrate that forgetting and collapse are strongly related, and different continual learning strategies help models preserve both capacity and performance in different efficiency.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

catastrophic forgetting评估通常通过任务准确性进行，但这种方法忽略了模型内部结构的变化。结构性坍塌（structural collapse）导致网络的可塑性降低，表现为有效秩（eRank）的变化，使得网络在学习新任务时失去扩展特征空间的能力，这迫使网络覆盖现有表示。为了研究遗忘与结构坍塌之间的关系，研究人员测量了权重和激活的eRank，发现两者之间存在密切联系。不同连续学习策略有助于模型在不同效率下保持容量和性能，例如SGD、LwF和ER策略分别用于训练MLP、ConvGRU、ResNet-18和Bi-ConvGRU等模型。这些评估表明，遗忘和结构坍塌之间存在密切联系，理解这一关系有助于开发更有效的连续学习策略。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • catastrophic forgetting评估通常通过任务准确性进行，但忽略了模型内部结构。
  • structural collapse导致网络的可塑性降低，表现为有效秩（eRank）的变化。
  • networks在学习新任务时失去扩展特征空间的能力，这迫使网络覆盖现有表示。
  • weight和activation eRank的测量有助于研究遗忘与结构坍塌之间的关系。
  • 不同连续学习策略有助于模型在不同效率下保持容量和性能。
  • MLP, ConvGRU, ResNet-18, Bi-ConvGRU在不同基准上进行了评估。
  • SGD, LwF, ER策略分别用于训练这些模型。
  • 遗忘和结构坍塌之间存在密切联系。

10. When to restart? Exploring escalating restarts on convergence

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04117v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Learning rate scheduling plays a critical role in the optimization of deep neural networks, directly influencing convergence speed, stability, and generalization. While existing schedulers such as cosine annealing, cyclical learning rates, and warm restarts have shown promise, they often rely on fixed or periodic triggers that are agnostic to the training dynamics, such as stagnation or convergence behavior. In this work, we propose a simple yet effective strategy, which we call Stochastic Gradient Descent with Escalating Restarts (SGD-ER). It adaptively increases the learning rate upon convergence. Our method monitors training progress and triggers restarts when stagnation is detected, linearly escalating the learning rate to escape sharp local minima and explore flatter regions of the loss landscape. We evaluate SGD-ER across CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and TinyImageNet on a range of architectures including ResNet-18/34/50, VGG-16, and DenseNet-101. Compared to standard schedulers, SGD-ER improves test accuracy by 0.5-4.5%, demonstrating the benefit of convergence-aware escalating restarts for better local optima.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，随着重启次数的增加，模型能够更有效地逃离尖锐的局部最小值，从而提高整体性能。其次，固定或周期性触发器可能无法准确捕捉训练动力学，导致训练过程中的停滞被忽视。此外，标准调度器往往难以适应这种停滞，进一步加剧了问题。因此，SGD-ER（随机梯度下降增强重启）通过检测训练过程中的停滞来触发重启，从而有效解决了这一问题。此外，SGD-ER在不同数据集和架构上表现出色，测试准确性的提升也证明了其在收敛感知重启方面的价值。因此，SGD-ER不仅能够提高模型的性能，还能确保训练过程更加稳定和高效。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • escalating restarts有助于逃离尖锐的局部最小值。
  • 固定或周期性触发器可能忽视训练动力学。
  • 标准调度器可能无法适应训练过程中的停滞。
  • SGD-ER通过检测停滞来触发重启。
  • SGD-ER在不同数据集和架构上表现出色。
  • 测试准确性提升表明了收敛感知重启的价值。

11. WTHaar-Net: a Hybrid Quantum-Classical Approach

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02497v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Convolutional neural networks rely on linear filtering operations that can be reformulated efficiently in suitable transform domains. At the same time, advances in quantum computing have shown that certain structured linear transforms can be implemented with shallow quantum circuits, opening the door to hybrid quantum-classical approaches for enhancing deep learning models. In this work, we introduce WTHaar-Net, a convolutional neural network that replaces the Hadamard Transform used in prior hybrid architectures with the Haar Wavelet Transform (HWT). Unlike the Hadamard Transform, the Haar transform provides spatially localized, multi-resolution representations that align more closely with the inductive biases of vision tasks. We show that the HWT admits a quantum realization using structured Hadamard gates, enabling its decomposition into unitary operations suitable for quantum circuits. Experiments on CIFAR-10 and Tiny-ImageNet demonstrate that WTHaar-Net achieves substantial parameter reduction while maintaining competitive accuracy. On Tiny-ImageNet, our approach outperforms both ResNet and Hadamard-based baselines. We validate the quantum implementation on IBM Quantum clo
  • 易漏细节梳理：

Haar变换提供空间局部化和多分辨率表示，这更符合视觉任务的归纳偏置，因此它在图像处理中具有优势。WTHaar-Net通过使用Haar小波变换替代哈达玛变换实现了参数减少，从而在Tiny-ImageNet上表现出色，优于ResNet和基于哈达玛变换的基线。此外，Haar变换的量子实现使用结构化的哈达玛门，便于分解为量子电路中的幺正操作，这使得WTHaar-Net在IBM量子云硬件上具有良好的兼容性。值得注意的是，Haar变换与哈达玛变换不同，后者不具备空间局部化特性，这也是选择Haar变换的原因之一。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • Haar变换提供空间局部化、多分辨率表示，更符合视觉任务的归纳偏置。
  • WTHaar-Net通过使用Haar小波变换替代哈达玛变换实现参数减少。
  • Haar变换的量子实现使用结构化的哈达玛门，便于分解为量子电路中的幺正操作。
  • WTHaar-Net在Tiny-ImageNet上的表现优于ResNet和基于哈达玛变换的基线。
  • 实验验证了WTHaar-Net在IBM量子云硬件上的兼容性。
  • Haar变换与哈达玛变换不同，后者不具备空间局部化特性。

12. On the Expressive Power of Transformers for Maxout Networks and Continuous Piecewise Linear Functions

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03084v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Transformer networks have achieved remarkable empirical success across a wide range of applications, yet their theoretical expressive power remains insufficiently understood. In this paper, we study the expressive capabilities of Transformer architectures. We first establish an explicit approximation of maxout networks by Transformer networks while preserving comparable model complexity. As a consequence, Transformers inherit the universal approximation capability of ReLU networks under similar complexity constraints. Building on this connection, we develop a framework to analyze the approximation of continuous piecewise linear functions by Transformers and quantitatively characterize their expressivity via the number of linear regions, which grows exponentially with depth. Our analysis establishes a theoretical bridge between approximation theory for standard feedforward neural networks and Transformer architectures. It also yields structural insights into Transformers: self-attention layers implement max-type operations, while feedforward layers realize token-wise affine transformations.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

maxout网络可以被Transformer网络显式逼近，这是因为Transformer继承了ReLU网络的通用逼近能力。自注意力层通过实现最大型操作，能够捕捉输入数据中的复杂关系，而前馈层则通过仿射变换实现令牌级别的线性变换。连续分段线性函数的逼近能力与Transformer的线性区域数量密切相关，而这一数量随深度呈指数增长。因此，Transformer的表达能力与标准前馈神经网络的逼近理论存在理论联系，这为理解其结构提供了新的视角。通过这些机制，Transformer能够更有效地逼近复杂的函数，展现出强大的表达能力。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • maxout网络可以被Transformer网络显式逼近。
  • Transformer继承了ReLU网络的通用逼近能力。
  • 自注意力层实现最大型操作。
  • 前馈层实现令牌级别的仿射变换。
  • 连续分段线性函数的逼近与Transformer的线性区域数量有关。
  • 线性区域数量随深度呈指数增长。
  • Transformer的表达能力与标准前馈神经网络的逼近理论存在理论联系。
  • Transformer的研究为理解其结构提供了新的视角。

13. Detecting Heads using Feature Refine Net and Cascaded Multi-Scale Architecture

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/1803.09256v4
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：This paper presents a method that can accurately detect heads especially small heads under the indoor scene. To achieve this, we propose a novel method, Feature Refine Net (FRN), and a cascaded multi-scale architecture. FRN exploits the multi-scale hierarchical features created by deep convolutional neural networks. The proposed channel weighting method enables FRN to make use of features alternatively and effectively. To improve the performance of small head detection, we propose a cascaded multi-scale architecture which has two detectors. One called global detector is responsible for detecting large objects and acquiring the global distribution information. The other called local detector is designed for small objects detection and makes use of the information provided by global detector. Due to the lack of head detection datasets, we have collected and labeled a new large dataset named SCUT-HEAD which includes 4405 images with 111251 heads annotated. Experiments show that our method has achieved state-of-the-art performance on SCUT-HEAD.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

FRN能够有效利用多尺度特征，通过通道加权方法实现特征的交替使用，从而提升检测性能。其中，全球检测器负责大物体的检测和全局信息的获取，而局部检测器则依赖于全球检测器提供的信息进行小物体的检测，特别是小头部的检测。然而，缺乏专门的头部检测数据集，使得小头部的检测成为一大挑战。幸运的是，SCUT-HEAD数据集的引入填补了这一空白，它包含4405张图像和111251个标注的头部，为小头部的检测提供了丰富的数据支持。因此，多尺度架构通过两个检测器的协同工作，显著提升了小头部的检测性能，并在SCUT-HEAD数据集上达到了最先进的性能。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • FRN能有效利用多尺度特征。
  • FRN通过通道加权方法实现特征的交替使用。
  • 全球检测器负责大物体检测和全局信息获取。
  • 局部检测器依赖于全球检测器提供的信息进行小物体检测。
  • 缺乏专门的头部检测数据集。
  • SCUT-HEAD数据集包含4405张图像和111251个标注的头部。
  • 该方法在SCUT-HEAD数据集上达到了最先进的性能。
  • 多尺度架构通过两个检测器协同工作提升小头部检测性能。

14. Parallel Test-Time Scaling with Multi-Sequence Verifiers

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03417v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Parallel test-time scaling, which generates multiple candidate solutions for a single problem, is a powerful technique for improving large language model performance. However, it is hindered by two key bottlenecks: accurately selecting the correct solution from the candidate pool, and the high inference latency from generating many full solutions. We argue that both challenges are fundamentally linked to verifier calibration. A well-calibrated verifier not only improves answer selection, but also enables early-stopping strategies to reduce latency. However, existing verifiers are limited as they score each candidate in isolation, overlooking rich contextual information across the set of candidates. To address this, we introduce the Multi-Sequence Verifier (MSV), the first verifier designed to jointly process all candidate solutions and model their interactions. MSV achieves improved calibration, which directly enhances best-of-N selection performance. We further introduce a streaming MSV variant that empowers a novel early-stopping framework. Our novel framework fully leverages parallel decoding, which contrasts with the existing multi-sequence early exit works that decode sequence
  • 易漏细节梳理：

well-calibrated 验证器能够显著提升答案选择的准确性，并且通过引入早期停止策略来优化处理流程。然而，现有的验证器在评估每个候选答案时会忽略上下文信息，这限制了其性能。相比之下，MSV（多序列验证器）能够同时处理所有候选解决方案，并通过建模它们之间的相互作用来充分利用上下文信息。此外，MSV的流式变体还支持一种新颖的早期停止框架，这进一步提高了处理效率。同时，平行解码技术能够充分利用解码速度，显著降低延迟。相比之下，现有的多序列早期退出方法则会逐个解码序列，这会增加整体延迟。因此，MSV不仅能够保持与传统方法相同的准确性，还能将延迟降低至一半，从而在处理效率上展现出显著优势。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • well-calibrated verifier improves answer selection and enables early-stopping strategies
  • existing verifiers score each candidate in isolation, missing contextual information
  • MSV jointly processes all candidate solutions, modeling their interactions
  • streaming MSV variant supports a novel early-stopping framework
  • parallel decoding fully leverages decoding speed, reducing latency
  • existing multi-sequence early exit methods decode sequences one by one, increasing latency
  • MSV can achieve the same accuracy with half the latency of its counterparts

[2603.03417v1] Parallel Test-Time Scaling with Multi-Sequence Verifiers Computer Science > Cryptography and Security arXiv:2603.03417v1 (cs) [Submitted on 3 Mar 2026] Title: Parallel Test-Time Scaling with Multi-Sequence Verifiers Authors: Yegon Kim , Seungyoo Lee , Chaeyun Jang , Hyungi Lee , Juho Lee View a PDF of the paper titled Parallel Test-Time Scaling with Multi-Sequence Verifiers, by Yegon Kim and 4 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Parallel test-time scaling, which generates multiple candidate solutions for a single problem, is a powerful technique for improving large language model performance. However, it is hindered by two key bottlenecks: accurately selecting the correct solution from the candidate pool, and the high inference latency from generating many full solutions. We argue that both challenges are fundamentally linked to verifier calibration. A well-calibrated verifier not only improves answer selection, but also enables early-stopping strategies to reduce latency. However, existing verifiers are limited as they score each candidate in isolation, overlooking rich contextual information across the set of candidates. 15. Riemannian Geometry of Optimal Rebalancing in Dynamic Weight Automated Market Makers

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05326v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In Temporal Function Market Making (TFMM), a dynamic weight AMM pool rebalances from initial to final holdings by creating a series of arbitrage opportunities whose total cost depends on the weight trajectory taken. We show that the per-step arbitrage loss is the KL divergence between new and old weight vectors, meaning the Fisher--Rao metric is the natural Riemannian metric on the weight simplex. The loss-minimising interpolation under the leading-order expansion of this KL cost is SLERP (Spherical Linear Interpolation) in the Hellinger coordinates $η_i = \sqrt{w_i}$, i.e.\ a geodesic on the positive orthant of the unit sphere traversed at constant speed. The SLERP midpoint equals the (AM+GM)/normalise heuristic of prior work (Willetts & Harrington, 2024), so the heuristic lies on the geodesic. This identity holds for any number of tokens and any magnitude of weight change; using this link, all dyadic points on the geodesic can be reached by recursive AM-GM bisection without trigonometric functions. SLERP's relative sub-optimality on the full KL cost is proportional to the squared magnitude of the overall weight change and to $1/f^2$, where $f$ is the number of interpolation steps
  • 易漏细节梳理：

KL散度用于衡量新旧权重向量之间的差异，而Fisher--Rao度量则是权重单纯形上的自然黎曼度量。SLERP（Spherical Linear Interpolation）在Hellinger坐标系下进行球面线性插值，其相对次优性与整体权重变化的平方成正比，与插值步骤数的平方成反比。实际上，SLERP的相对次优性可以追溯到AM-GM（Arithmetic Mean-Geometric Mean）不等式的启发式方法，即AM-GM中点等同于先前工作的启发式方法。通过递归的AM-GM二分法，所有二进制点都可以被达到，这一结果适用于任意数量的代币和任意权重变化量。因此，通过这些方法，可以有效地处理权重向量的变化，确保在权重调整过程中保持一定的精度和效率。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • KL divergence衡量新旧权重向量之间的差异。
  • Fisher--Rao metric是权重单纯形上的自然黎曼度量。
  • SLERP是在Hellinger坐标下的球面线性插值。
  • SLERP的相对次优性与整体权重变化的平方成正比。
  • SLERP的相对次优性与插值步骤数的平方成反比。
  • AM-GM中点等同于先前工作的启发式方法。
  • 所有二进制点可以通过递归AM-GM二分法达到。
  • 该结果适用于任意数量的代币和任意权重变化量。

16. On the Rate of Convergence of GD in Non-linear Neural Networks: An Adversarial Robustness Perspective

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02095v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We study the convergence dynamics of Gradient Descent (GD) in a minimal binary classification setting, consisting of a two-neuron ReLU network and two training instances. We prove that even under these strong simplifying assumptions, while GD successfully converges to an optimal robustness margin, effectively maximizing the distance between the decision boundary and the training points, this convergence occurs at a prohibitively slow rate, scaling strictly as $Θ(1/\ln(t))$. To the best of our knowledge, this establishes the first explicit lower bound on the convergence rate of the robustness margin in a non-linear model. Through empirical simulations, we further demonstrate that this inherent failure mode is pervasive, exhibiting the exact same tight convergence rate across multiple natural network initializations. Our theoretical guarantees are derived via a rigorous analysis of the GD trajectories across the distinct activation patterns of the model. Specifically, we develop tight control over the system's dynamics to bound the trajectory of the decision boundary, overcoming the primary technical challenge introduced by the non-linear nature of the architecture.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

GD在非线性神经网络中的收敛速度非常慢，这一问题在多种网络初始化中普遍存在。首先，这种慢收敛现象可以通过理论分析来解释，具体来说，收敛速度严格地与1/ln(t)成正比。其次，这一慢收敛问题与网络的非线性性质直接相关，是由于非线性架构的主要技术挑战在于轨迹控制。此外，研究者通过分析GD轨迹在模型不同激活模式下的动态来推导出收敛率的下界，这是首次明确给出非线性模型鲁棒性边界的收敛率下界。因此，这些理论保证不仅揭示了非线性模型的收敛特性，还为理解非线性神经网络的鲁棒性提供了重要依据。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • GD在非线性神经网络中的收敛速度非常慢。
  • 收敛速度严格地与1/ln(t)成正比。
  • 这是首次明确给出非线性模型鲁棒性边界的收敛率下界。
  • 实验表明，这种收敛慢的问题在多种网络初始化中普遍存在。
  • 理论保证通过分析GD轨迹在模型不同激活模式下的动态来推导。
  • 非线性架构的主要技术挑战是轨迹控制。
  • 收敛慢的问题与网络的非线性性质直接相关。

[2603.02095v1] On the Rate of Convergence of GD in Non-linear Neural Networks: An Adversarial Robustness Perspective Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2603.02095v1 (cs) [Submitted on 2 Mar 2026] Title: On the Rate of Convergence of GD in Non-linear Neural Networks: An Adversarial Robustness Perspective Authors: Guy Smorodinsky , Sveta Gimpleson , Itay Safran View a PDF of the paper titled On the Rate of Convergence of GD in Non-linear Neural Networks: An Adversarial Robustness Perspective, by Guy Smorodinsky and Sveta Gimpleson and Itay Safran View PDF Abstract: We study the convergence dynamics of Gradient Descent (GD) in a minimal binary classification setting, consisting of a two-neuron ReLU network and two training instances. To the best of our knowledge, this establishes the first explicit lower bound on the convergence rate of the robustness margin in a non-linear model. Our theoretical guarantees are derived via a rigorous analysis of the GD trajectories across the distinct activation patterns of the model. Specifically, we develop tight control over the system's dynamics to bound the trajectory of the decision boundary, overcoming the primary technical challenge introduced by the non-linear nature of the architecture. 17. Fixed Anchors Are Not Enough: Dynamic Retrieval and Persistent Homology for Dataset Distillation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24144v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Decoupled dataset distillation (DD) compresses large corpora into a few synthetic images by matching a frozen teacher's statistics. However, current residual-matching pipelines rely on static real patches, creating a fit-complexity gap and a pull-to-anchor effect that reduce intra-class diversity and hurt generalization. To address these issues, we introduce RETA -- a Retrieval and Topology Alignment framework for decoupled DD. First, Dynamic Retrieval Connection (DRC) selects a real patch from a prebuilt pool by minimizing a fit-complexity score in teacher feature space; the chosen patch is injected via a residual connection to tighten feature fit while controlling injected complexity. Second, Persistent Topology Alignment (PTA) regularizes synthesis with persistent homology: we build a mutual k-NN feature graph, compute persistence images of components and loops, and penalize topology discrepancies between real and synthetic sets, mitigating pull-to-anchor effect. Across CIFAR-100, Tiny-ImageNet, ImageNet-1K, and multiple ImageNet subsets, RETA consistently outperforms various baselines under comparable time and memory, especially reaching 64.3% top-1 accuracy on ImageNet-1K with
  • 易漏细节梳理：

static real patches 与 fit-complexity gap 之间的关系导致了模型在内类多样性上的不足，具体表现为静态真实补丁与拟合复杂度之间的差距，这使得模型难以捕捉到足够的内在多样性。为了解决这一问题，DRC（动态补丁选择）通过在教师特征空间中最小化 fit-complexity 分数来优化补丁选择，从而通过残差连接选择的补丁进一步加强了特征拟合。此外，PTA（持久同调正则化合成）利用持久同调理论来正则化合成过程，通过构建互邻特征图和计算组件和循环的持久图像，进一步提高了模型的泛化能力。这种正则化方法有效地惩罚了真实集和合成集之间的拓扑差异，从而提高了模型的准确性。因此，RETA（实时拓扑正则化合成）在相似的时间和内存消耗下，取得了显著的性能提升，尤其是在 ImageNet-1K 数据集上的 top-1 准确率达到了 64.3%，相比之前的最佳方法，取得了 3.1% 的显著改进。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • static real patches create a fit-complexity gap
  • fit-complexity gap reduces intra-class diversity
  • pull-to-anchor effect hurts generalization
  • DRC minimizes fit-complexity score in teacher feature space
  • chosen patch via residual connection tightens feature fit
  • PTA uses persistent homology to regularize synthesis
  • mutual k-NN feature graph is built for PTA
  • persistence images of components and loops are computed
  • topology discrepancies between real and synthetic sets are penalized
  • RETA outperforms baselines under comparable time and memory
  • RETA reaches 64.3% top-1 accuracy on ImageNet-1K
  • +3.1% improvement over the best prior method

18. Differential Privacy in Two-Layer Networks: How DP-SGD Harms Fairness and Robustness

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04881v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Differentially private learning is essential for training models on sensitive data, but empirical studies consistently show that it can degrade performance, introduce fairness issues like disparate impact, and reduce adversarial robustness. The theoretical underpinnings of these phenomena in modern, non-convex neural networks remain largely unexplored. This paper introduces a unified feature-centric framework to analyze the feature learning dynamics of differentially private stochastic gradient descent (DP-SGD) in two-layer ReLU convolutional neural networks. Our analysis establishes test loss bounds governed by a crucial metric: the feature-to-noise ratio (FNR). We demonstrate that the noise required for privacy leads to suboptimal feature learning, and specifically show that: 1) imbalanced FNRs across classes and subpopulations cause disparate impact; 2) even in the same class, noise has a greater negative impact on semantically long-tailed data; and 3) noise injection exacerbates vulnerability to adversarial attacks. Furthermore, our analysis reveals that the popular paradigm of public pre-training and private fine-tuning does not guarantee improvement, particularly under signif
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，差分隐私虽然能保护数据隐私，但可能会降低模型性能。其次，不平衡的特征噪声比例会导致不同的影响，特别是在数据集之间特征与噪声的比例差异较大时，这种影响更为显著。此外，噪声的注入使得模型更容易受到对抗性攻击的影响，尤其是对于语义上长尾数据，噪声的影响更为显著。因此，仅仅依赖公共预训练和私人微调并不能保证模型性能的提升。最后，不同数据集之间的特征分布变化会降低模型的鲁棒性，进一步加剧了模型性能的不稳定性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • differential privacy can degrade model performance.
  • imbalanced feature-to-noise ratios cause disparate impact.
  • noise has a greater negative impact on semantically long-tailed data.
  • noise injection makes models more vulnerable to adversarial attacks.
  • public pre-training and private fine-tuning do not guarantee improvement.
  • feature distribution shifts between datasets can reduce model robustness.

[2603.04881v1] Differential Privacy in Two-Layer Networks: How DP-SGD Harms Fairness and Robustness Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2603.04881v1 (cs) [Submitted on 5 Mar 2026] Title: Differential Privacy in Two-Layer Networks: How DP-SGD Harms Fairness and Robustness Authors: Ruichen Xu , Kexin Chen View a PDF of the paper titled Differential Privacy in Two-Layer Networks: How DP-SGD Harms Fairness and Robustness, by Ruichen Xu and 1 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Differentially private learning is essential for training models on sensitive data, but empirical studies consistently show that it can degrade performance, introduce fairness issues like disparate impact, and reduce adversarial robustness. The theoretical underpinnings of these phenomena in modern, non-convex neural networks remain largely unexplored. This paper introduces a unified feature-centric framework to analyze the feature learning dynamics of differentially private stochastic gradient descent (DP-SGD) in two-layer ReLU convolutional neural networks. 19. ResGene-T: A Tensor-Based Residual Network Approach for Genomic Prediction

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.00744v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In this work, we propose a new deep learning model for Genomic Prediction (GP), which involves correlating genotypic data with phenotypic. The genotypes are typically fed as a sequence of characters to the 1D-Convolution Neural Network layer of the underlying deep learning model. Inspired by earlier work that represented genotype as a 2D-image for genotype-phenotype classification, we extend this idea to GP, which is a regression task. We use a ResNet-18 as the underlying architecture, and term this model as ResGene-2D. Although the 2D-image representation captures biological interactions well, it requires all the layers of the model to do so. This limits training efficiency. Thus, as seen in the earlier work that proposed a 2D-image representation, our ResGene-2D performs almost the same as other models (3% improvement). To overcome this, we propose a novel idea of converting the 2D-image into a 3D/ tensor and feed this to the ResNet-18 architecture, and term this model as ResGene-T. We evaluate our proposed models on three crop species having ten phenotypic traits and compare it with seven most popular models (two statistical, two machine learning, and three deep learning). R
  • 易漏细节梳理：

D-图像表示要求所有模型层捕捉生物相互作用，这限制了ResGene-2D模型的训练效率。相比之下，ResGene-T模型采用3D/张量表示，不仅能够更好地利用ResNet-18架构的能力，还提高了训练效率和性能。具体来说，ResGene-T在基因组预测任务中表现最佳，相较于其他模型，其性能提升了3%，并在不同基因型数据的复杂性方面表现出色。ResGene-T通过将基因型转换为3D/张量，能够更有效地捕捉复杂的相互作用，从而在三种作物物种的十种表型特征评估中表现出色，其性能提升范围从14.51%到41.51%不等。因此，ResGene-T的设计旨在将基因组预测任务视为回归问题，其优越性能归因于基于张量的表示方法，而2D-图像表示则可能无法充分利用ResNet-18架构的潜力，也无法完全捕捉基因型数据的深度和复杂性。综上所述，ResGene-T的张量基表示方法不仅提高了模型的训练效率，还提供了更准确、更全面的基因型表示，从而在基因组预测任务中提供了更稳健和详尽的解决方案。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • D-image representation requires all model layers to capture biological interactions.
  • This limits the training efficiency of the ResGene-2D model.
  • ResGene-T model uses a 3D/tensor representation to improve training efficiency.
  • ResGene-T performs the best among the compared models for genomic prediction tasks.
  • The 2D-image representation does not fully utilize the ResNet-18 architecture's capabilities.
  • ResGene-T achieves 3% improvement over other models with the same architecture.
  • The 3D/tensor representation helps in capturing complex interactions more effectively.

20. Mixture of Universal Experts: Scaling Virtual Width via Depth-Width Transformation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04971v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) decouples model capacity from per-token computation, yet their scalability remains limited by the physical dimensions of depth and width. To overcome this, we propose Mixture of Universal Experts (MOUE),a MoE generalization introducing a novel scaling dimension: Virtual Width. In general, MoUE aims to reuse a universal layer-agnostic expert pool across layers, converting depth into virtual width under a fixed per-token activation budget. However, two challenges remain: a routing path explosion from recursive expert reuse, and a mismatch between the exposure induced by reuse and the conventional load-balancing objectives. We address these with three core components: a Staggered Rotational Topology for structured expert sharing, a Universal Expert Load Balance for depth-aware exposure correction, and a Universal Router with lightweight trajectory state for coherent multi-step routing. Empirically, MoUE consistently outperforms matched MoE baselines by up to 1.3% across scaling regimes, enables progressive conversion of existing MoE checkpoints with up to 4.2% gains, and reveals a new scaling dimension for MoE architectures.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

路由路径爆炸是由于递归重用专家导致的，这给多专家统一扩展（MOUE）带来了挑战。同时，由于重用引起的暴露与传统的负载均衡目标之间存在不匹配，这也是MOUE面临的一个问题。为了解决这些问题，设计了交错旋转拓扑结构，以促进结构化的专家共享。此外，通用专家负载平衡有助于纠正深度感知的暴露，而通用路由器则通过轻量级轨迹状态确保连贯的多步骤路由。这些改进使得MOUE在与匹配的MOUE基线相比时，表现得更为出色，最多可提高1.3%。更进一步，MOUE还能够逐步将现有的MOE检查点转换为具有高达4.2%收益的新模型。虚拟宽度作为MOE架构的一个新的扩展维度，为解决这些问题提供了新的视角。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • routing path explosion from recursive expert reuse is a challenge for MOUE.
  • mismatch between exposure induced by reuse and conventional load-balancing objectives is another challenge for MOUE.
  • staggered rotational topology helps with structured expert sharing.
  • universal expert load balance aids in depth-aware exposure correction.
  • universal router with lightweight trajectory state enables coherent multi-step routing.
  • moue consistently outperforms matched moe baselines by up to 1.3%.
  • moue enables progressive conversion of existing moe checkpoints with up to 4.2% gains.
  • virtual width is a new scaling dimension for moe architectures.
  • routing path explosion occurs due to recursive reuse of experts.
  • exposure induced by reuse can differ from load-balancing objectives.
  • staggered rotational topology is designed for structured sharing.
  • universal expert load balance corrects depth-aware exposure.
  • universal router ensures coherent multi-step routing.

To overcome this, we propose Mixture of Universal Experts (MOUE),a MoE generalization introducing a novel scaling dimension: Virtual Width. In general, MoUE aims to reuse a universal layer-agnostic expert pool across layers, converting depth into virtual width under a fixed per-token activation budget. However, two challenges remain: a routing path explosion from recursive expert reuse, and a mismatch between the exposure induced by reuse and the conventional load-balancing objectives. We address these with three core components: a Staggered Rotational Topology for structured expert sharing, a Universal Expert Load Balance for depth-aware exposure correction, and a Universal Router with lightweight trajectory state for coherent multi-step routing. Empirically, MoUE consistently outperforms matched MoE baselines by up to 1.3% across scaling regimes, enables progressive conversion of existing MoE checkpoints with up to 4.2% gains, and reveals a new scaling dimension for MoE architectures. 21. Temporal Pooling Strategies for Training-Free Anomalous Sound Detection with Self-Supervised Audio Embeddings

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04605v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Training-free anomalous sound detection (ASD) based on pre-trained audio embedding models has recently garnered significant attention, as it enables the detection of anomalous sounds using only normal reference data while offering improved robustness under domain shifts. However, existing embedding-based approaches almost exclusively rely on temporal mean pooling, while alternative pooling strategies have so far only been explored for spectrogram-based representations. Consequently, the role of temporal pooling in training-free ASD with pre-trained embeddings remains insufficiently understood. In this paper, we present a systematic evaluation of temporal pooling strategies across multiple state-of-the-art audio embedding models. We propose relative deviation pooling (RDP), an adaptive pooling method that emphasizes informative temporal deviations, and introduce a hybrid pooling strategy that combines RDP with generalized mean pooling. Experiments on five benchmark datasets demonstrate that the proposed methods consistently outperform mean pooling and achieve state-of-the-art performance for training-free ASD, including results that surpass all previously reported trained systems an
  • 易漏细节梳理：

在现有的基于嵌入的方法中，时间平均池化是主导策略，但在预训练音频嵌入中，替代的时间池化策略尚未得到广泛探索。时间池化在无训练的自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）检测中扮演着至关重要的但尚未完全理解的角色。相对偏差池化（RDP）强调了具有信息性的时域偏差，而提出的混合池化方法结合了RDP与广义平均池化。实验结果表明，这些新方法在性能上优于时间平均池化，其结果超越了所有之前报告的训练系统和集成在DCASE2025 ASD数据集上的表现。时间池化策略在多个最先进的音频嵌入模型中得到了评估，无训练的ASD能够仅使用正常参考数据检测异常声音，更好地处理领域偏移。因此，时间池化仍然是预训练音频嵌入模型中一个关键但尚未充分研究的方面。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • temporal mean pooling is the predominant strategy in existing embedding-based approaches.
  • alternative pooling strategies have not been extensively explored for pre-trained audio embeddings.
  • temporal pooling plays a crucial but under-understood role in training-free ASD with pre-trained embeddings.
  • relative deviation pooling (RDP) emphasizes informative temporal deviations.
  • hybrid pooling combining RDP with generalized mean pooling is proposed.
  • experiments demonstrate that proposed methods outperform mean pooling.
  • results surpass all previously reported trained systems and ensembles on the DCASE2025 ASD dataset.
  • temporal pooling strategies are evaluated across multiple state-of-the-art audio embedding models.
  • training-free ASD enables detection of anomalous sounds using only normal reference data.
  • domain shifts are better handled by training-free ASD.
  • temporal pooling remains a critical but understudied aspect in pre-trained audio embedding models.

22. How Does the ReLU Activation Affect the Implicit Bias of Gradient Descent on High-dimensional Neural Network Regression?

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04895v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Overparameterized ML models, including neural networks, typically induce underdetermined training objectives with multiple global minima. The implicit bias refers to the limiting global minimum that is attained by a common optimization algorithm, such as gradient descent (GD). In this paper, we characterize the implicit bias of GD for training a shallow ReLU model with the squared loss on high-dimensional random features. Prior work showed that the implicit bias does not exist in the worst-case (Vardi and Shamir, 2021), or corresponds exactly to the minimum-l2-norm solution among all global minima under exactly orthogonal data (Boursier et al., 2022). Our work interpolates between these two extremes and shows that, for sufficiently high-dimensional random data, the implicit bias approximates the minimum-l2-norm solution with high probability with a gap on the order $Θ(\sqrt{n/d})$, where n is the number of training examples and d is the feature dimension. Our results are obtained through a novel primal-dual analysis, which carefully tracks the evolution of predictions, data-span coefficients, as well as their interactions, and shows that the ReLU activation pattern quickly stabiliz

[2603.04895v1] How Does the ReLU Activation Affect the Implicit Bias of Gradient Descent on High-dimensional Neural Network Regression? Statistics > Machine Learning arXiv:2603.04895v1 (stat) [Submitted on 5 Mar 2026] Title: How Does the ReLU Activation Affect the Implicit Bias of Gradient Descent on High-dimensional Neural Network Regression? Authors: Kuo-Wei Lai , Guanghui Wang , Molei Tao , Vidya Muthukumar View a PDF of the paper titled How Does the ReLU Activation Affect the Implicit Bias of Gradient Descent on High-dimensional Neural Network Regression?, by Kuo-Wei Lai and 3 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Overparameterized ML models, including neural networks, typically induce underdetermined training objectives with multiple global minima. The implicit bias refers to the limiting global minimum that is attained by a common optimization algorithm, such as gradient descent (GD). In this paper, we characterize the implicit bias of GD for training a shallow ReLU model with the squared loss on high-dimensional random features. Prior work showed that the implicit bias does not exist in the worst-case (Vardi and Shamir, 2021), or corresponds exactly to the minimum-l2-norm solution among all global minima under exactly orthogonal data (Boursier et al., 2022). Our results are obtained through a novel primal-dual analysis, which carefully tracks the evolution of predictions, data-span coefficients, as well as their interactions, and shows that the ReLU activation pattern quickly stabilizes with high probability over the random data. 23. Smoothness Adaptivity in Constant-Depth Neural Networks: Optimal Rates via Smooth Activations

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.19691v2
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Smooth activation functions are ubiquitous in modern deep learning, yet their theoretical advantages over non-smooth counterparts remain poorly understood. In this work, we study both approximation and statistical properties of neural networks with smooth activations for learning functions in the Sobolev space $W^{s,\infty}([0,1]^d)$ with $s>0$. We prove that constant-depth networks equipped with smooth activations achieve smoothness adaptivity: increasing width alone suffices to attain the minimax-optimal approximation and estimation error rates (up to logarithmic factors). In contrast, for non-smooth activations such as ReLU, smoothness adaptivity is fundamentally limited by depth: the attainable approximation order is bounded by depth, and higher-order smoothness requires proportional depth growth. These results identify activation smoothness as a fundamental mechanism, complementary to depth, for achieving optimal rates over Sobolev function classes. Technically, our analysis is based on a multi-scale approximation framework that yields explicit neural network approximators with controlled parameter norms and model size. This complexity control ensures statistical learnability
  • 易漏细节梳理：

smoothness adaptivity 依赖于激活函数的平滑性，而不仅仅是网络的深度。常深网络通过使用平滑激活函数实现了平滑度适应性，即仅通过增加宽度即可达到最优的逼近和估计误差率。相比之下，非平滑激活函数如ReLU无法通过增加宽度实现高阶平滑度，因此需要深度增长。尽管平滑激活函数的理论优势尚未完全理解，但它们在现代深度学习中非常普遍，并有助于避免先前分析中常见的不可行的$\ell^0$稀疏性约束。平深网络的分析基于多尺度逼近框架，确保了在经验风险最小化下的统计可学习性。平滑激活函数不仅有助于实现索伯列夫函数类的最优率，还补充了深度学习机制，使其在逼近复杂函数时更具优势。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • smoothness adaptivity 依赖于激活函数的平滑性，而不仅仅是网络的深度。
  • 常深网络使用平滑激活函数可以实现平滑度适应性，即仅通过增加宽度即可达到最优的逼近和估计误差率。
  • 非平滑激活函数如ReLU无法通过增加宽度实现高阶平滑度，需要深度增长。
  • 平滑激活函数的理论优势尚未完全理解，但它们在现代深度学习中非常普遍。
  • 平滑激活函数的使用有助于避免先前分析中常见的不可行的$\ell^0$稀疏性约束。
  • 平深网络的分析基于多尺度逼近框架，确保了在经验风险最小化下的统计可学习性。
  • 平滑激活函数有助于实现索伯列夫函数类的最优率，是深度的一种补充机制。

[2602.19691v2] Smoothness Adaptivity in Constant-Depth Neural Networks: Optimal Rates via Smooth Activations Statistics > Machine Learning arXiv:2602.19691v2 (stat) [Submitted on 23 Feb 2026 ( v1 ), last revised 28 Feb 2026 (this version, v2)] Title: Smoothness Adaptivity in Constant-Depth Neural Networks: Optimal Rates via Smooth Activations Authors: Yuhao Liu , Zilin Wang , Lei Wu , Shaobo Zhang View a PDF of the paper titled Smoothness Adaptivity in Constant-Depth Neural Networks: Optimal Rates via Smooth Activations, by Yuhao Liu and 3 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Smooth activation functions are ubiquitous in modern deep learning, yet their theoretical advantages over non-smooth counterparts remain poorly understood. 24. Deepfake Word Detection by Next-token Prediction using Fine-tuned Whisper

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22658v2
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Deepfake speech utterances can be forged by replacing one or more words in a bona fide utterance with semantically different words synthesized with speech-generative models. While a dedicated synthetic word detector could be developed, we developed a cost-effective method that fine-tunes a pre-trained Whisper model to detect synthetic words while transcribing the input utterance via next-token prediction. We further investigate using partially vocoded utterances as the fine-tuning data, thus reducing the cost of data collection. Our experiments demonstrate that, on in-domain test data, the fine-tuned Whisper yields low synthetic-word detection error rates and transcription error rates. On out-of-domain test data with synthetic words produced with unseen speech-generative models, the fine-tuned Whisper remains on par with a dedicated ResNet-based detection model; however, the overall performance degradation calls for strategies to improve its generalization capability.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

fine-tuned Whisper模型通过依赖于下一个词预测的方法，实现了成本效益的训练。部分 vocoded 语音数据的使用不仅减少了数据收集成本，还确保了模型在in-domain测试数据上的低错误率。尽管在out-of-domain测试数据上，fine-tuned Whisper的表现与专用ResNet模型相当，但整体性能的下降提示我们需要采取策略来提高模型的泛化能力。此外，fine-tuned Whisper在检测由未见过的语音生成模型创建的合成词方面也表现出成本效益。在转写方面，该模型同样表现出低错误率。因此，为了进一步提升模型的性能，研究团队应关注泛化能力的提升，并考虑使用更多样化的数据进行训练。提交给Interspeech的论文应包含提交信息，而arXiv发行的DOI则通过DataCite提供，提交历史记录则显示了论文的版本信息。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • fine-tuned Whisper模型的成本效益方法依赖于下一个词预测。
  • 部分 vocoded 语音数据的使用减少了数据收集成本。
  • in-domain 测试数据上，fine-tuned Whisper表现出低错误率。
  • out-of-domain 测试数据上，fine-tuned Whisper与专用 ResNet 模型表现相当。
  • 整体性能下降表明需要提高泛化能力的策略。
  • fine-tuned Whisper在检测合成词方面具有成本效益。
  • 合成词由未见过的语音生成模型创建。
  • 数据收集成本通过使用部分 vocoded 数据降低。
  • fine-tuned Whisper在转写方面也表现出低错误率。

25. GRAIL: Post-hoc Compensation by Linear Reconstruction for Compressed Networks

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23795v2
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Structured deep model compression methods are hardware-friendly and substantially reduce memory and inference costs. However, under aggressive compression, the resulting accuracy degradation often necessitates post-compression finetuning, which can be impractical due to missing labeled data or high training cost. We propose post-hoc blockwise compensation, called GRAIL, a simple zero-finetuning step applied after model compression that restores each block's input-output behavior using a small calibration set. The method summarizes hidden activations via a Gram matrix and applies ridge regression to linearly reconstruct the original hidden representation from the reduced one. The resulting reconstruction map is absorbed into the downstream projection weights, while the upstream layer is compressed. The approach is selector-agnostic (Magnitude, Wanda, Gram-based selection, or folding), data-aware (requiring only a few forward passes without gradients or labels), and recovers classic pruning or folding when the Gram matrix is near identity, indicating weak inter-channel correlations. Across ResNets, ViTs, and decoder-only LLMs, GRAIL consistently improves accuracy or perplexity over d
  • 易漏细节梳理：

post-hoc finetuning 方法可能因缺乏标注数据或高训练成本而变得 impractical，因此它在实际应用中可能不太可行。然而，当 Gram matrix 近似于单位矩阵时，该方法可以恢复经典剪枝或折叠操作，从而提供一种有效的替代方案。此外，reconstruction map 能够吸收进下游投影权重，而上游层则被压缩，使得整个网络结构更加紧凑。值得注意的是，该方法对选择器是 agnostic 的，可以适用于 Magnitude、Wanda、Gram 等不同基准选择或折叠操作。由于仅需少量前向传递，无需梯度或标签，因此该方法是 data-aware 的，具有较低的数据依赖性。压缩后的网络在实际压缩范围内能够一致地提高准确度或困惑度，且具有可管理的开销，无需反向传播。此外，相关代码已开源，可以在 GitHub 上获取。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • post-hoc finetuning 可能因缺乏标注数据或高训练成本而 impractical。
  • Gram matrix 近似于单位矩阵时，方法可恢复经典剪枝或折叠操作。
  • reconstruction map 吸收进下游投影权重，而上游层被压缩。
  • 方法对选择器 agnostic，对 Magnitude、Wanda、Gram 基准选择或折叠都适用。
  • 仅需少量前向传递，无需梯度或标签，方法是 data-aware。
  • 压缩后的网络在实际压缩范围内能一致提高准确度或困惑度。
  • 该方法具有可管理的开销，无需反向传播。
  • code 可在 GitHub 上获取。

[2602.23795v2] GRAIL: Post-hoc Compensation by Linear Reconstruction for Compressed Networks Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2602.23795v2 (cs) [Submitted on 27 Feb 2026 ( v1 ), last revised 2 Mar 2026 (this version, v2)] Title: GRAIL: Post-hoc Compensation by Linear Reconstruction for Compressed Networks Authors: Wenwu Tang , Dong Wang , Lothar Thiele , Olga Saukh View a PDF of the paper titled GRAIL: Post-hoc Compensation by Linear Reconstruction for Compressed Networks, by Wenwu Tang and 3 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Structured deep model compression methods are hardware-friendly and substantially reduce memory and inference costs. However, under aggressive compression, the resulting accuracy degradation often necessitates post-compression finetuning, which can be impractical due to missing labeled data or high training cost. We propose post-hoc blockwise compensation, called GRAIL, a simple zero-finetuning step applied after model compression that restores each block's input-output behavior using a small calibration set. The method summarizes hidden activations via a Gram matrix and applies ridge regression to linearly reconstruct the original hidden representation from the reduced one. The resulting reconstruction map is absorbed into the downstream projection weights, while the upstream layer is compressed. The approach is selector-agnostic (Magnitude, Wanda, Gram-based selection, or folding), data-aware (requiring only a few forward passes without gradients or labels), and recovers classic pruning or folding when the Gram matrix is near identity, indicating weak inter-channel correlations. Across ResNets, ViTs, and decoder-only LLMs, GRAIL consistently improves accuracy or perplexity over data-free and data-aware pruning or folding baselines in practical compression regimes, with manageable overhead and no backpropagation. The code is available at this https URL . 26. MLOps-Assisted Anomalous Reflector Metasurfaces Design Based on Red Hat OpenShift AI

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03981v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The integration of artificial intelligence as a design tool for metasurfaces, and the implementation of a deep-learning model pose a challenge in the development of an automated solution due to high resources requirements. The presented work introduces a network-layer solution to configure such environment for end user objectives, and for an underlying physical-layer technology. An architecture is developed to design an anomalous reflector by employing the Redhat Openshift AI (RHOAI) technology to support an automated machine learning operations (MLOps) framework in smart radio environments. This entails the design of lossless impenetrable metasurfaces characterized by a scalar surface impedance for an optimal anomalous reflection, achieved by optimizing the number of the Floquet modes through the utilization of a local power conservation constraint qualified as a fitness function. The metasurfaces design process is implemented by using a conditional generative adversarial network (cGAN). An extended cGAN with a surrogate model assists in a high-quality freeform metasurfaces design, where it introduces a swift simulation tool for the metasurfaces design process and analysis of the
  • 易漏细节梳理：

自动化解决方案需要高资源要求，因此网络层解决方案被用于配置自动化环境，以确保高效运行。物理层技术需要进一步优化，以满足高资源需求。为了解决这一问题，Redhat Openshift AI被引入，以支持MLOps框架，从而提高系统的灵活性和可扩展性。此外，Floquet模式的优化有助于实现最优异常反射，进一步提升系统的性能。在设计无损不可穿透的元表面时，cGAN被用于生成所需的模型，而模拟工具则加速了元表面的设计过程。训练准确性证明了在容器化环境中部署的可行性，这也表明了Redhat Openshift AI在实际应用中的有效性。尽管如此，系统构建仍然面临挑战，需要潜在的抽象层来简化复杂性，提高系统的整体效率。因此，通过优化资源要求、引入先进的技术和工具，以及构建潜在的抽象层，可以有效解决这些挑战，推动系统的持续改进和发展。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 自动化解决方案需要高资源要求。
  • 网络层解决方案用于配置自动化环境。
  • 物理层技术需要优化。
  • 使用Redhat Openshift AI支持MLOps框架。
  • 优化Floquet模式以实现最优异常反射。
  • cGAN用于设计无损不可穿透的元表面。
  • 模拟工具加速元表面设计过程。
  • 训练准确性证明了部署在容器化环境中的可行性。
  • ResNet-50在文献中的其他部署被提及。
  • 系统构建面临挑战，需要潜在的抽象层。

27. A Multi-Dimensional Quality Scoring Framework for Decentralized LLM Inference with Proof of Quality

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04028v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Decentralized large language model (LLM) inference networks can pool heterogeneous compute to scale serving, but they require lightweight and incentive-compatible mechanisms to assess output quality. Prior work introduced cost-aware Proof of Quality (PoQ) and adaptive robust PoQ to allocate rewards under evaluator heterogeneity and adversarial behavior. In this paper, we focus on the quality signal itself and propose a multi-dimensional quality scoring framework that decomposes output quality into modular dimensions, including model and cost priors, structure quality, semantic quality, query-output alignment, and agreement/uncertainty. Using logged outputs from QA and summarization tasks, we systematically audit dimension reliability and show that seemingly reasonable dimensions can be task-dependent and even negatively correlated with reference quality without calibration. While the default composite underperforms a strong single semantic evaluator, ablations reveal that removing unreliable dimensions and re-normalizing weights yields a calibrated composite that matches or exceeds the best single- evaluator and consensus baselines. Finally, we integrate the composite score as a dr
  • 易漏细节梳理：

multi-dimensional质量评分框架将输出质量分解为多个模块化维度，这些维度可能任务依赖且未经校准会与参考质量负相关。dimension可靠性审计进一步揭示，看似合理的维度可能因任务而异且未经校准同样会与参考质量负相关。默认组合评分表现不佳，但通过去除不可靠维度并重新归一化权重，可以得到校准的组合评分，该评分能够匹配或超越最佳单一评估器和共识基线。集成复合评分作为PoQ的即插即用质量信号，展示了鲁棒聚合和适应性信任加权的互补益处。在评估器攻击下，这些方法还能提供额外的好处，从而增强整体质量信号的鲁棒性和可靠性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • multi-dimensional quality scoring框架将输出质量分解为多个模块化维度，需注意这些维度可能任务依赖且未经校准会与参考质量负相关。
  • dimension可靠性审计显示，看似合理的维度可能因任务而异且未经校准会与参考质量负相关。
  • 默认组合评分表现不佳，但通过去除不可靠维度并重新归一化权重，可获得校准的组合评分，匹配或超越最佳单一评估器和共识基线。

  • 评估器攻击下，鲁棒聚合和适应性信任加权能提供额外的好处。

[2603.04028v1] A Multi-Dimensional Quality Scoring Framework for Decentralized LLM Inference with Proof of Quality Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2603.04028v1 (cs) [Submitted on 4 Mar 2026] Title: A Multi-Dimensional Quality Scoring Framework for Decentralized LLM Inference with Proof of Quality Authors: Arther Tian , Alex Ding , Frank Chen , Simon Wu , Aaron Chan View a PDF of the paper titled A Multi-Dimensional Quality Scoring Framework for Decentralized LLM Inference with Proof of Quality, by Arther Tian and 4 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Decentralized large language model (LLM) inference networks can pool heterogeneous compute to scale serving, but they require lightweight and incentive-compatible mechanisms to assess output quality. Prior work introduced cost-aware Proof of Quality (PoQ) and adaptive robust PoQ to allocate rewards under evaluator heterogeneity and adversarial behavior. In this paper, we focus on the quality signal itself and propose a multi-dimensional quality scoring framework that decomposes output quality into modular dimensions, including model and cost priors, structure quality, semantic quality, query-output alignment, and agreement/uncertainty. Using logged outputs from QA and summarization tasks, we systematically audit dimension reliability and show that seemingly reasonable dimensions can be task-dependent and even negatively correlated with reference quality without calibration. While the default composite underperforms a strong single semantic evaluator, ablations reveal that removing unreliable dimensions and re-normalizing weights yields a calibrated composite that matches or exceeds the best single- evaluator and consensus baselines. Finally, we integrate the composite score as a drop-in quality signal in PoQ and demonstrate complementary benefits with robust aggregation and adaptive trust weighting under adversarial evaluator attacks. 28. Quantitative Approximation Rates for Group Equivariant Learning

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.20370v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The universal approximation theorem establishes that neural networks can approximate any continuous function on a compact set. Later works in approximation theory provide quantitative approximation rates for ReLU networks on the class of $α$-Hölder functions $f: [0,1]^N \to \mathbb{R}$. The goal of this paper is to provide similar quantitative approximation results in the context of group equivariant learning, where the learned $α$-Hölder function is known to obey certain group symmetries. While there has been much interest in the literature in understanding the universal approximation properties of equivariant models, very few quantitative approximation results are known for equivariant models. In this paper, we bridge this gap by deriving quantitative approximation rates for several prominent group-equivariant and invariant architectures. The architectures that we consider include: the permutation-invariant Deep Sets architecture; the permutation-equivariant Sumformer and Transformer architectures; joint invariance to permutations and rigid motions using invariant networks based on frame averaging; and general bi-Lipschitz invariant models. Overall, we show that equally-sized R
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，神经网络能够逼近任何连续函数，尽管具体逼近速率依赖于函数的性质。其次，定量逼近结果对于ReLU网络在α-Holder函数类上的逼近已经有所研究。然而，本论文的目标是在群等变学习的背景下提供类似的定量逼近结果。尽管等变模型的普遍逼近性质在文献中受到了广泛关注，但定量逼近结果却相对较少。因此，本文推导了几种重要等变和不变架构的定量逼近速率，包括置换不变的Deep Sets架构、置换等变的Sumformer和Transformer架构，以及联合置换和刚性运动不变性。此外，等变模型和同等大小的ReLU MLP在等变函数上具有相同的表达能力，硬编码等变性不会导致这些模型表达能力和逼近能力的损失。因此，这些定量逼近结果为等变模型在实际应用中的性能提供了理论支持。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 神经网络可以逼近任何连续函数，但具体逼近速率依赖于函数的性质。
  • 定量逼近结果对于ReLU网络在α-Holder函数类上是已知的。
  • 本论文的目标是在群等变学习的背景下提供类似的定量逼近结果。
  • 等变模型的普遍逼近性质在文献中受到了广泛关注，但定量逼近结果很少。
  • 本文推导了几种重要等变和不变架构的定量逼近速率。
  • 考虑的架构包括置换不变的Deep Sets架构。
  • 考虑的架构还包括置换等变的Sumformer和Transformer架构。
  • 考虑的架构还包括联合置换和刚性运动不变性。
  • 等变模型和同等大小的ReLU MLP在等变函数上具有相同的表达能力。
  • 硬编码等变性不会导致这些模型表达能力和逼近能力的损失。

[2602.20370v1] Quantitative Approximation Rates for Group Equivariant Learning Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2602.20370v1 (cs) [Submitted on 23 Feb 2026] Title: Quantitative Approximation Rates for Group Equivariant Learning Authors: Jonathan W. Siegel , Snir Hordan , Hannah Lawrence , Ali Syed , Nadav Dym View a PDF of the paper titled Quantitative Approximation Rates for Group Equivariant Learning, by Jonathan W. Siegel and Snir Hordan and Hannah Lawrence and Ali Syed and Nadav Dym View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: The universal approximation theorem establishes that neural networks can approximate any continuous function on a compact set. Later works in approximation theory provide quantitative approximation rates for ReLU networks on the class of $\alpha$-Hölder functions $f: [0,1]^N \to \mathbb{R}$. The goal of this paper is to provide similar quantitative approximation results in the context of group equivariant learning, where the learned $\alpha$-Hölder function is known to obey certain group symmetries. While there has been much interest in the literature in understanding the universal approximation properties of equivariant models, very few quantitative approximation results are known for equivariant models. In this paper, we bridge this gap by deriving quantitative approximation rates for several prominent group-equivariant and invariant architectures. The architectures that we consider include: the permutation-invariant Deep Sets architecture; the permutation-equivariant Sumformer and Transformer architectures; joint invariance to permutations and rigid motions using invariant networks based on frame averaging; and general bi-Lipschitz invariant models. Overall, we show that equally-sized ReLU MLPs and equivariant architectures are equally expressive over equivariant functions. Thus, hard-coding equivariance does not result in a loss of expressivity or approximation power in these models. 29. DeepAFL: Deep Analytic Federated Learning

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.00579v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Federated Learning (FL) is a popular distributed learning paradigm to break down data silo. Traditional FL approaches largely rely on gradient-based updates, facing significant issues about heterogeneity, scalability, convergence, and overhead, etc. Recently, some analytic-learning-based work has attempted to handle these issues by eliminating gradient-based updates via analytical (i.e., closed-form) solutions. Despite achieving superior invariance to data heterogeneity, these approaches are fundamentally limited by their single-layer linear model with a frozen pre-trained backbone. As a result, they can only achieve suboptimal performance due to their lack of representation learning capabilities. In this paper, to enable representable analytic models while preserving the ideal invariance to data heterogeneity for FL, we propose our Deep Analytic Federated Learning approach, named DeepAFL. Drawing inspiration from the great success of ResNet in gradient-based learning, we design gradient-free residual blocks in our DeepAFL with analytical solutions. We introduce an efficient layer-wise protocol for training our deep analytic models layer by layer in FL through least squares. Both t
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，基于梯度的更新方法容易遇到异质性和可扩展性的问题。其次，分析学习方法能够更好地保持对数据异质性的不变性。然而，单一层的线性模型缺乏表示学习的能力。为此，DeepAFL引入了无梯度残差块，增强了表示学习。此外，通过最小二乘法进行逐层训练的协议提高了训练效率。因此，DeepAFL在三个基准数据集上超越了最先进的基线方法。异质性不变性和表示学习是DeepAFL的双重优势。ResNet的成功设计启发了DeepAFL中无梯度残差块的设计。高效的逐层训练协议进一步提升了DeepAFL的性能。最后，理论分析和实验评估验证了DeepAFL的优越性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • gradient-based updates are prone to issues like heterogeneity and scalability.
  • analytic-learning-based approaches can achieve better invariance to data heterogeneity.
  • single-layer linear models lack representation learning capabilities.
  • gradient-free residual blocks enhance representation learning in DeepAFL.
  • layer-wise protocol through least squares improves training efficiency.
  • DeepAFL outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in three benchmark datasets.
  • heterogeneity invariance and representation learning are DeepAFL's dual advantages.
  • ResNet's success inspires the design of gradient-free residual blocks in DeepAFL.
  • efficient layer-wise training protocol contributes to DeepAFL's performance.
  • theoretical analyses and empirical evaluations validate DeepAFL's superiority.

[2603.00579v1] DeepAFL: Deep Analytic Federated Learning Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2603.00579v1 (cs) [Submitted on 28 Feb 2026] Title: DeepAFL: Deep Analytic Federated Learning Authors: Jianheng Tang , Yajiang Huang , Kejia Fan , Feijiang Han , Jiaxu Li , Jinfeng Xu , Run He , Anfeng Liu , Houbing Herbert Song , Huiping Zhuang , Yunhuai Liu View a PDF of the paper titled DeepAFL: Deep Analytic Federated Learning, by Jianheng Tang and 10 other authors View PDF Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) is a popular distributed learning paradigm to break down data silo. Traditional FL approaches largely rely on gradient-based updates, facing significant issues about heterogeneity, scalability, convergence, and overhead, etc. Recently, some analytic-learning-based work has attempted to handle these issues by eliminating gradient-based updates via analytical (i.e., closed-form) solutions. Despite achieving superior invariance to data heterogeneity, these approaches are fundamentally limited by their single-layer linear model with a frozen pre-trained backbone. As a result, they can only achieve suboptimal performance due to their lack of representation learning capabilities. In this paper, to enable representable analytic models while preserving the ideal invariance to data heterogeneity for FL, we propose our Deep Analytic Federated Learning approach, named DeepAFL. Drawing inspiration from the great success of ResNet in gradient-based learning, we design gradient-free residual blocks in our DeepAFL with analytical solutions. We introduce an efficient layer-wise protocol for training our deep analytic models layer by layer in FL through least squares. Both theoretical analyses and empirical evaluations validate our DeepAFL's superior performance with its dual advantages in heterogeneity invariance and representation learning, outperforming state-of-the-art baselines by up to 5.68%-8.42% across three benchmark datasets. 30. Physics-consistent deep learning for blind aberration recovery in mobile optics

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04999v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Mobile photography is often limited by complex, lens-specific optical aberrations. While recent deep learning methods approach this as an end-to-end deblurring task, these "black-box" models lack explicit optical modeling and can hallucinate details. Conversely, classical blind deconvolution remains highly unstable. To bridge this gap, we present Lens2Zernike, a deep learning framework that blindly recovers physical optical parameters from a single blurred image. To the best of our knowledge, no prior work has simultaneously integrated supervision across three distinct optical domains. We introduce a novel physics-consistent strategy that explicitly minimizes errors via direct Zernike coefficient regression (z), differentiable physics constraints encompassing both wavefront and point spread function derivations (p), and auxiliary multi-task spatial map predictions (m). Through an ablation study on a ResNet-18 backbone, we demonstrate that our full multi-task framework (z+p+m) yields a 35% improvement over coefficient-only baselines. Crucially, comparative analysis reveals that our approach outperforms two established deep learning methods from previous literature, achieving signifi
  • 易漏细节梳理：

black-box 模型由于缺乏显式的光学建模，可能会生成虚假细节，这直接影响了图像的质量。为了解决这一问题，研究者采用了Zernike系数回归直接最小化误差的方法，这种方法提供了一种物理一致的策略，有助于生成更真实的图像。此外，不同的物理约束，如波前和点扩展函数的导数，也被引入以进一步优化模型。为了提高整体性能，研究者还引入了辅助多任务空间图预测，这有助于更好地捕捉图像中的细节。相比之下，系数基线方法在性能上无法与引入的多任务框架相媲美。最终，通过恢复的物理参数，该方法不仅使非盲去模糊更加稳定，还显著改善了图像质量。因此，该方法在专利数据库上的表现优于现有技术，展示了其在实际应用中的优越性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • black-box 模型缺乏显式的光学建模，可能会生成虚假细节。
  • Zernike系数回归直接最小化误差，提供了一种物理一致的策略。
  • 不同的物理约束包括波前和点扩展函数的导数。
  • 辅助多任务空间图预测有助于提高整体性能。
  • 系数基线方法无法与引入的多任务框架相媲美。
  • 恢复的物理参数使非盲去模糊稳定，显著改善了图像质量。
  • 该方法在专利数据库上的表现优于现有技术。

[2603.04999v1] Physics-consistent deep learning for blind aberration recovery in mobile optics Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2603.04999v1 (cs) [Submitted on 5 Mar 2026] Title: Physics-consistent deep learning for blind aberration recovery in mobile optics Authors: Kartik Jhawar , Tamo Sancho Miguel Tandoc , Khoo Jun Xuan , Wang Lipo View a PDF of the paper titled Physics-consistent deep learning for blind aberration recovery in mobile optics, by Kartik Jhawar and 3 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Mobile photography is often limited by complex, lens-specific optical aberrations. While recent deep learning methods approach this as an end-to-end deblurring task, these "black-box" models lack explicit optical modeling and can hallucinate details. Conversely, classical blind deconvolution remains highly unstable. To bridge this gap, we present Lens2Zernike, a deep learning framework that blindly recovers physical optical parameters from a single blurred image. To the best of our knowledge, no prior work has simultaneously integrated supervision across three distinct optical domains. We introduce a novel physics-consistent strategy that explicitly minimizes errors via direct Zernike coefficient regression (z), differentiable physics constraints encompassing both wavefront and point spread function derivations (p), and auxiliary multi-task spatial map predictions (m). Through an ablation study on a ResNet-18 backbone, we demonstrate that our full multi-task framework (z+p+m) yields a 35% improvement over coefficient-only baselines. Crucially, comparative analysis reveals that our approach outperforms two established deep learning methods from previous literature, achieving significantly lower regression errors. Ultimately, we demonstrate that these recovered physical parameters enable stable non-blind deconvolution, providing substantial in-domain improvement on the patented Institute for Digital Molecular Analytics and Science (IDMxS) Mobile Camera Lens Database for restoring diffraction-limited details from severely aberrated mobile captures. 31. Embracing Events and Frames with Hierarchical Feature Refinement Network for Object Detection

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2407.12582v2
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In frame-based vision, object detection faces substantial performance degradation under challenging conditions due to the limited sensing capability of conventional cameras. Event cameras output sparse and asynchronous events, providing a potential solution to solve these problems. However, effectively fusing two heterogeneous modalities remains an open issue. In this work, we propose a novel hierarchical feature refinement network for event-frame fusion. The core concept is the design of the coarse-to-fine fusion module, denoted as the cross-modality adaptive feature refinement (CAFR) module. In the initial phase, the bidirectional cross-modality interaction (BCI) part facilitates information bridging from two distinct sources. Subsequently, the features are further refined by aligning the channel-level mean and variance in the two-fold adaptive feature refinement (TAFR) part. We conducted extensive experiments on two benchmarks: the low-resolution PKU-DDD17-Car dataset and the high-resolution DSEC dataset. Experimental results show that our method surpasses the state-of-the-art by an impressive margin of $\textbf{8.0}\%$ on the DSEC dataset. Besides, our method exhibits significa
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，coarse-to-fine 融合模块通过逐步细化特征，提升了融合效果，为整个网络奠定了基础。其次，bidirectional cross-modality 交互机制有助于不同模态之间的信息互通，进一步增强了特征的综合能力。此外，TAFR 部分通过对齐通道级均值和方差，进一步细化特征，确保了特征的准确性和一致性。CAFR 模块作为整个网络的核心，负责跨模态特征的适应性细化，确保了不同模态之间的无缝融合。实验在低分辨率和高分辨率数据集上进行，验证了方法的有效性。引入不同类型的图像腐蚀，展示了方法的鲁棒性提升，使其在面对多种图像腐蚀时表现更稳定，鲁棒性提高显著。因此，提出的网络在 DSEC 数据集上超越了现有方法 8.0%，展示了其在实际应用中的优越性能。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • coarse-to-fine 融合模块能逐步细化特征，提升融合效果。
  • bidirectional cross-modality 交互有助于不同模态之间的信息互通。
  • TAFR 部分通过对齐通道级均值和方差进一步细化特征。
  • CAFR 模块是整个网络的核心，负责跨模态特征的适应性细化。
  • 实验在低分辨率和高分辨率数据集上进行，验证了方法的有效性。
  • 引入不同类型的图像腐蚀，展示了方法的鲁棒性提升。
  • 提出的网络在 DSEC 数据集上超越了现有方法 8.0%。
  • 方法在面对多种图像腐蚀时表现更稳定，鲁棒性提高显著。
