[2407.12582v2] Embracing Events and Frames with Hierarchical Feature Refinement Network for Object Detection Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2407.12582v2 (cs) [Submitted on 17 Jul 2024 ( v1 ), last revised 31 Oct 2024 (this version, v2)] Title: Embracing Events and Frames with Hierarchical Feature Refinement Network for Object Detection Authors: Hu Cao , Zehua Zhang , Yan Xia , Xinyi Li , Jiahao Xia , Guang Chen , Alois Knoll View a PDF of the paper titled Embracing Events and Frames with Hierarchical Feature Refinement Network for Object Detection, by Hu Cao and 6 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: In frame-based vision, object detection faces substantial performance degradation under challenging conditions due to the limited sensing capability of conventional cameras. Event cameras output sparse and asynchronous events, providing a potential solution to solve these problems. However, effectively fusing two heterogeneous modalities remains an open issue. In this work, we propose a novel hierarchical feature refinement network for event-frame fusion. The core concept is the design of the coarse-to-fine fusion module, denoted as the cross-modality adaptive feature refinement (CAFR) module. In the initial phase, the bidirectional cross-modality interaction (BCI) part facilitates information bridging from two distinct sources. Subsequently, the features are further refined by aligning the channel-level mean and variance in the two-fold adaptive feature refinement (TAFR) part. We conducted extensive experiments on two benchmarks: the low-resolution PKU-DDD17-Car dataset and the high-resolution DSEC dataset. Experimental results show that our method surpasses the state-of-the-art by an impressive margin of $\textbf{8.0}\%$ on the DSEC dataset. Besides, our method exhibits significantly better robustness (\textbf{69.5}\% versus \textbf{38.7}\%) when introducing 15 different corruption types to the frame images. The code can be found at the link ( this https URL ). 32. Omni-Manip: Beyond-FOV Large-Workspace Humanoid Manipulation with Omnidirectional 3D Perception

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05355v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The deployment of humanoid robots for dexterous manipulation in unstructured environments remains challenging due to perceptual limitations that constrain the effective workspace. In scenarios where physical constraints prevent the robot from repositioning itself, maintaining omnidirectional awareness becomes far more critical than color or semantic information. While recent advances in visuomotor policy learning have improved manipulation capabilities, conventional RGB-D solutions suffer from narrow fields of view (FOV) and self-occlusion, requiring frequent base movements that introduce motion uncertainty and safety risks. Existing approaches to expanding perception, including active vision systems and third-view cameras, introduce mechanical complexity, calibration dependencies, and latency that hinder reliable real-time performance. In this work, We propose Omni-Manip, an end-to-end LiDAR-driven 3D visuomotor policy that enables robust manipulation in large workspaces. Our method processes panoramic point clouds through a Time-Aware Attention Pooling mechanism, efficiently encoding sparse 3D data while capturing temporal dependencies. This 360° perception allows the robot to in
  • 易漏细节梳理：

窄视野（FOV）限制了机器人的有效工作空间，而自遮挡问题进一步加剧了传统RGB-D解决方案的局限性。频繁的基座移动引入了运动不确定性，并增加了安全风险。为了解决这些问题，引入了主动视觉系统和第三视角摄像头，但这也增加了机械复杂性。此外，校准依赖性和延迟阻碍了实时性能。在这种情况下，全方位的感知比颜色或语义信息更为关键，因为它允许机器人在无需频繁重新定位的情况下进行交互。时间感知的注意力池化能够高效地编码稀疏的3D数据，而全身远程操作则支持在全身协调方面进行高效的数据收集。现有的方法在处理机械复杂性和延迟方面存在困难，而全方位的3D感知在大工作空间场景中则表现出色，超越了基准方法。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • narrow fields of view (FOV) limit the robot's effective workspace.
  • self-occlusion issues exacerbate the limitations of conventional RGB-D solutions.
  • frequent base movements introduce motion uncertainty and safety risks.
  • active vision systems and third-view cameras add mechanical complexity.
  • calibration dependencies and latency hinder real-time performance.
  • omnidirectional awareness is more critical than color or semantic information.
  • ° perception allows the robot to interact without frequent repositioning.
  • time-aware attention pooling efficiently encodes sparse 3D data.
  • whole-body teleoperation supports efficient data collection on full-body coordination.
  • existing approaches struggle with mechanical complexity and latency.
  • omni-directional 3D perception outperforms baselines in large-workspace scenarios.

[2603.05355v1] Omni-Manip: Beyond-FOV Large-Workspace Humanoid Manipulation with Omnidirectional 3D Perception Computer Science > Robotics arXiv:2603.05355v1 (cs) [Submitted on 5 Mar 2026] Title: Omni-Manip: Beyond-FOV Large-Workspace Humanoid Manipulation with Omnidirectional 3D Perception Authors: Pei Qu , Zheng Li , Yufei Jia , Ziyun Liu , Liang Zhu , Haoang Li , Jinni Zhou , Jun Ma View a PDF of the paper titled Omni-Manip: Beyond-FOV Large-Workspace Humanoid Manipulation with Omnidirectional 3D Perception, by Pei Qu and 7 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: The deployment of humanoid robots for dexterous manipulation in unstructured environments remains challenging due to perceptual limitations that constrain the effective workspace. In scenarios where physical constraints prevent the robot from repositioning itself, maintaining omnidirectional awareness becomes far more critical than color or semantic information. While recent advances in visuomotor policy learning have improved manipulation capabilities, conventional RGB-D solutions suffer from narrow fields of view (FOV) and self-occlusion, requiring frequent base movements that introduce motion uncertainty and safety risks. Existing approaches to expanding perception, including active vision systems and third-view cameras, introduce mechanical complexity, calibration dependencies, and latency that hinder reliable real-time performance. In this work, We propose Omni-Manip, an end-to-end LiDAR-driven 3D visuomotor policy that enables robust manipulation in large workspaces. Our method processes panoramic point clouds through a Time-Aware Attention Pooling mechanism, efficiently encoding sparse 3D data while capturing temporal dependencies. This 360° perception allows the robot to interact with objects across wide areas without frequent repositioning. To support policy learning, we develop a whole-body teleoperation system for efficient data collection on full-body coordination. Extensive experiments in simulation and real-world environments show that Omni-Manip achieves robust performance in large-workspace and cluttered scenarios, outperforming baselines that rely on egocentric depth cameras. 33. TLU-Net: A Deep Learning Approach for Automatic Steel Surface Defect Detection

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2101.06915v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Visual steel surface defect detection is an essential step in steel sheet manufacturing. Several machine learning-based automated visual inspection (AVI) methods have been studied in recent years. However, most steel manufacturing industries still use manual visual inspection due to training time and inaccuracies involved with AVI methods. Automatic steel defect detection methods could be useful in less expensive and faster quality control and feedback. But preparing the annotated training data for segmentation and classification could be a costly process. In this work, we propose to use the Transfer Learning-based U-Net (TLU-Net) framework for steel surface defect detection. We use a U-Net architecture as the base and explore two kinds of encoders: ResNet and DenseNet. We compare these nets' performance using random initialization and the pre-trained networks trained using the ImageNet data set. The experiments are performed using Severstal data. The results demonstrate that the transfer learning performs 5% (absolute) better than that of the random initialization in defect classification. We found that the transfer learning performs 26% (relative) better than that of the random i
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，迁移学习能够显著提高缺陷检测的性能，这主要是因为预训练网络比随机初始化网络更快地实现收敛。其次，缺陷分类的性能提升相对较小，仅为5%的绝对值增长。相比之下，缺陷分割的性能提升更为显著，达到了26%的相对值增长。此外，较少的训练数据也能进一步提升迁移学习的效果，使得模型在有限的数据条件下依然能够取得较好的性能。因此，迁移学习在缺陷检测中具有重要的应用潜力，能够有效提升检测的准确性和效率。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • transfer learning可以提高缺陷检测的性能。
  • 缺陷分类的性能提升为5%（绝对值）。
  • 缺陷分割的性能提升为26%（相对值）。
  • 预训练网络比随机初始化网络收敛更快。
  • 较少的训练数据可以进一步提升迁移学习的效果。
  • 迁移学习在缺陷检测中具有应用潜力。

[2101.06915v1] TLU-Net: A Deep Learning Approach for Automatic Steel Surface Defect Detection Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2101.06915v1 (cs) [Submitted on 18 Jan 2021] Title: TLU-Net: A Deep Learning Approach for Automatic Steel Surface Defect Detection Authors: Praveen Damacharla , Achuth Rao M. V. , Jordan Ringenberg , Ahmad Y Javaid View a PDF of the paper titled TLU-Net: A Deep Learning Approach for Automatic Steel Surface Defect Detection, by Praveen Damacharla and 3 other authors View PDF Abstract: Visual steel surface defect detection is an essential step in steel sheet manufacturing. Several machine learning-based automated visual inspection (AVI) methods have been studied in recent years. However, most steel manufacturing industries still use manual visual inspection due to training time and inaccuracies involved with AVI methods. Automatic steel defect detection methods could be useful in less expensive and faster quality control and feedback. But preparing the annotated training data for segmentation and classification could be a costly process. In this work, we propose to use the Transfer Learning-based U-Net (TLU-Net) framework for steel surface defect detection. We use a U-Net architecture as the base and explore two kinds of encoders: ResNet and DenseNet. We compare these nets' performance using random initialization and the pre-trained networks trained using the ImageNet data set. The experiments are performed using Severstal data. The results demonstrate that the transfer learning performs 5% (absolute) better than that of the random initialization in defect classification. We found that the transfer learning performs 26% (relative) better than that of the random initialization in defect segmentation. We also found the gain of transfer learning increases as the training data decreases, and the convergence rate with transfer learning is better than that of the random initialization. 34. Why ReLU? A Bit-Model Dichotomy for Deep Network Training

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.19017v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Theoretical analyses of Empirical Risk Minimization (ERM) are standardly framed within the Real-RAM model of computation. In this setting, training even simple neural networks is known to be $\exists \mathbb{R}$-complete -- a complexity class believed to be harder than NP, that characterizes the difficulty of solving systems of polynomial inequalities over the real numbers. However, this algebraic framework diverges from the reality of digital computation with finite-precision hardware. In this work, we analyze the theoretical complexity of ERM under a realistic bit-level model ($\mathsf{ERM}{\text{bit}}$), where network parameters and inputs are constrained to be rational numbers with polynomially bounded bit-lengths. Under this model, we reveal a sharp dichotomy in tractability governed by the network's activation function. We prove that for deep networks with {\em any} polynomial activations with rational coefficients and degree at least $2$, the bit-complexity of training is severe: deciding $\mathsf{ERM}}$ is $#P$-Hard, hence believed to be strictly harder than NP-complete problems. Furthermore, we show that determining the sign of a single partial derivative of
  • 易漏细节梳理：

训练在实数机（Real-RAM模型）下的问题被认为是$\exists \mathbb{R}$-完全的，这意味着这类问题非常困难。决定$\mathsf{ERM}_{\text{bit}}$（基于比特的错误最小化）是$\#P$-Hard的，这表明计算特定样本的损失函数的精确值是极其复杂的。此外，确定单个偏导数的符号也是不可行的，进一步凸显了计算的难度。决定梯度中的某个特定比特是$\#P$-Hard的，这表明在有限精度约束下，学习变得非常困难。尽管如此，对于ReLU激活函数的$\mathsf{ERM}_{\text{bit}}$问题被包含在NP中，而标准的反向传播算法对于ReLU是运行在多项式时间内的。$\exists \mathbb{R}$-完全问题被认为比NP类更难，而$\#P$-Hard问题则被认为比NP-完全类更难。因此，学习的可计算性二分性取决于网络的激活函数，而现实中的比特级模型揭示了不同激活函数之间的复杂性差异。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • training in the Real-RAM model is $\exists \mathbb{R}$-complete.
  • deciding $\mathsf{ERM}_{\text{bit}}$ is $\#P$-Hard.
  • determining the sign of a single partial derivative is intractable.
  • deciding a specific bit in the gradient is $\#P$-Hard.
  • finite-precision constraints are fundamental to learnability.
  • $\mathsf{ERM}_{\text{bit}}$ for ReLU is contained within NP.
  • standard backpropagation for ReLU runs in polynomial time.
  • $\exists \mathbb{R}$-complete problems are believed to be harder than NP.
  • $\#P$-Hard problems are believed to be strictly harder than NP-complete.
  • tractability dichotomy depends on the network's activation function.
  • realistic bit-level model reveals complexity differences between activations.

[2602.19017v1] Why ReLU? A Bit-Model Dichotomy for Deep Network Training Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2602.19017v1 (cs) [Submitted on 22 Feb 2026] Title: Why ReLU? A Bit-Model Dichotomy for Deep Network Training Authors: Ilan Doron-Arad , Elchanan Mossel View a PDF of the paper titled Why ReLU? A Bit-Model Dichotomy for Deep Network Training, by Ilan Doron-Arad and Elchanan Mossel View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Theoretical analyses of Empirical Risk Minimization (ERM) are standardly framed within the Real-RAM model of computation. In this setting, training even simple neural networks is known to be $\exists \mathbb{R}$-complete -- a complexity class believed to be harder than NP, that characterizes the difficulty of solving systems of polynomial inequalities over the real numbers. However, this algebraic framework diverges from the reality of digital computation with finite-precision hardware. In this work, we analyze the theoretical complexity of ERM under a realistic bit-level model ($\mathsf{ERM}{\text{bit}}$), where network parameters and inputs are constrained to be rational numbers with polynomially bounded bit-lengths. Under this model, we reveal a sharp dichotomy in tractability governed by the network's activation function. We prove that for deep networks with {\em any} polynomial activations with rational coefficients and degree at least $2$, the bit-complexity of training is severe: deciding $\mathsf{ERM}}$ is $#P$-Hard, hence believed to be strictly harder than NP-complete problems. Furthermore, we show that determining the sign of a single partial derivative of the empirical loss function is intractable (unlikely in BPP), and deciding a specific bit in the gradient is $#P$-Hard. This provides a complexity-theoretic perspective for the phenomenon of exploding and vanishing gradients. In contrast, we show that for piecewise-linear activations such as ReLU, the precision requirements remain manageable: $\mathsf{ERM}_{\text{bit}}$ is contained within NP (specifically NP-complete), and standard backpropagation runs in polynomial time. Our results demonstrate that finite-precision constraints are not merely implementation details but fundamental determinants of learnability. 35. Deep Learning-Based Meat Freshness Detection with Segmentation and OOD-Aware Classification

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.00368v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In this study, we present a meat freshness classification framework from Red-Green-Blue (RGB) images that supports both packaged and unpackaged meat datasets. The system classifies four in-distribution (ID) meat classes and uses an out-of-distribution (OOD)-aware abstention mechanism that flags low-confidence samples as No Result. The pipeline combines U-Net-based segmentation with deep feature classifiers. Segmentation is used as a preprocessing step to isolate the meat region and reduce background, producing more consistent inputs for classification. The segmentation module achieved an Intersection over Union (IoU) of 75% and a Dice coefficient of 82%, producing standardized inputs for the classification stage. For classification, we benchmark five backbones: Residual Network-50 (ResNet-50), Vision Transformer-Base/16 (ViT-B/16), Swin Transformer-Tiny (Swin-T), EfficientNet-B0, and MobileNetV3-Small. We use nested 5x3 cross-validation (CV) for model selection and hyperparameter tuning. On the held-out ID test set, EfficientNet-B0 achieves the highest accuracy (98.10%), followed by ResNet-50 and MobileNetV3-Small (both 97.63%) and Swin-T (97.51%), while ViT-B/16 is lower (94.42%).
  • 易漏细节梳理：

OOD-aware机制会将低置信度样本标记为No Result，这有助于提高模型的鲁棒性。IoU为75%，Dice系数为82%，表明分割模块表现良好，这为后续的分类任务奠定了基础。在ID测试集上，EfficientNet-B0表现最佳，而ViT-B/16的表现较差，Swin-T则介于两者之间。ResNet-50和MobileNetV3-Small在ID测试集上的表现相近，这表明不同的模型架构在特定任务上具有相似的性能。为了确保模型选择和超参数调整的准确性，使用了交叉验证。在设备上，通过TFLite进行实时检测，以实现高效的推理。此外，OOD评估使用标准的OOD指标，确保模型在面对未见过的样本时也能保持良好的性能。分割步骤有助于提高分类的一致性，从而进一步提升整体模型的可靠性。因此，通过这些措施，可以确保模型在实际应用中的稳定性和准确性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • OOD-aware机制会将低置信度样本标记为No Result。
  • IoU为75%，Dice系数为82%，表明分割模块表现良好。
  • EfficientNet-B0在ID测试集上表现最佳。
  • ViT-B/16在ID测试集上的表现较差。
  • Swin-T在ID测试集上的表现介于其他模型之间。
  • ResNet-50和MobileNetV3-Small在ID测试集上的表现相近。
  • 交叉验证用于模型选择和超参数调整。
  • 在设备上使用TFLite进行实时检测。
  • OOD评估使用标准OOD指标。
  • 报告了模型的实时延迟。
  • 分割步骤有助于提高分类的一致性。

[2603.00368v1] Deep Learning-Based Meat Freshness Detection with Segmentation and OOD-Aware Classification Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2603.00368v1 (cs) [Submitted on 27 Feb 2026] Title: Deep Learning-Based Meat Freshness Detection with Segmentation and OOD-Aware Classification Authors: Hutama Arif Bramantyo , Mukarram Ali Faridi , Rui Chen , Clarissa Harris , Yin Sun View a PDF of the paper titled Deep Learning-Based Meat Freshness Detection with Segmentation and OOD-Aware Classification, by Hutama Arif Bramantyo and 4 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: In this study, we present a meat freshness classification framework from Red-Green-Blue (RGB) images that supports both packaged and unpackaged meat datasets. The system classifies four in-distribution (ID) meat classes and uses an out-of-distribution (OOD)-aware abstention mechanism that flags low-confidence samples as No Result. The pipeline combines U-Net-based segmentation with deep feature classifiers. Segmentation is used as a preprocessing step to isolate the meat region and reduce background, producing more consistent inputs for classification. The segmentation module achieved an Intersection over Union (IoU) of 75% and a Dice coefficient of 82%, producing standardized inputs for the classification stage. For classification, we benchmark five backbones: Residual Network-50 (ResNet-50), Vision Transformer-Base/16 (ViT-B/16), Swin Transformer-Tiny (Swin-T), EfficientNet-B0, and MobileNetV3-Small. We use nested 5x3 cross-validation (CV) for model selection and hyperparameter tuning. On the held-out ID test set, EfficientNet-B0 achieves the highest accuracy (98.10%), followed by ResNet-50 and MobileNetV3-Small (both 97.63%) and Swin-T (97.51%), while ViT-B/16 is lower (94.42%). We additionally evaluate OOD scoring and thresholding using standard OOD metrics and sensitivity analysis over the abstention threshold. Finally, we report on-device latency using TensorFlow Lite (TFLite) on a smartphone, highlighting practical accuracy-latency trade-offs for future deployment. 36. Feature Decomposition and Reconstruction Learning for Effective Facial Expression Recognition

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2104.05160v2
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In this paper, we propose a novel Feature Decomposition and Reconstruction Learning (FDRL) method for effective facial expression recognition. We view the expression information as the combination of the shared information (expression similarities) across different expressions and the unique information (expression-specific variations) for each expression. More specifically, FDRL mainly consists of two crucial networks: a Feature Decomposition Network (FDN) and a Feature Reconstruction Network (FRN). In particular, FDN first decomposes the basic features extracted from a backbone network into a set of facial action-aware latent features to model expression similarities. Then, FRN captures the intra-feature and inter-feature relationships for latent features to characterize expression-specific variations, and reconstructs the expression feature. To this end, two modules including an intra-feature relation modeling module and an inter-feature relation modeling module are developed in FRN. Experimental results on both the in-the-lab databases (including CK+, MMI, and Oulu-CASIA) and the in-the-wild databases (including RAF-DB and SFEW) show that the proposed FDRL method consistently a
  • 易漏细节梳理：

FDRL方法通过分解和重构特征来提高面部表情识别的准确性，具体而言，FDN网络首先将基本特征分解为面部动作感知的潜在特征，以建模表情相似性，而FRN网络则进一步捕捉这些潜在特征的内部关系和外部关系，以表征表情特定的变化。这种方法在实验室数据库和野外数据库上均表现出色，证明了其有效性和实用性。然而，特征分解和重构对分类表情有益，但常见误解是认为它只是简单的特征提取，实际上，FDRL方法通过深入挖掘特征间的内在联系，实现了更精细的表情识别。因此，特征分解和重构不仅仅是简单的特征提取，而是通过建模和表征表情的复杂变化，提高了识别的准确性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • FDRL方法通过分解和重构特征来提高面部表情识别的准确性。
  • FDN网络首先将基本特征分解为面部动作感知的潜在特征，以建模表情相似性。
  • FRN网络捕捉潜在特征的内部关系和外部关系，以表征表情特定的变化。
  • FDRL方法在实验室数据库和野外数据库上均表现出色。
  • 特征分解和重构对分类表情有益，但常见误解是认为它只是简单的特征提取。

We view the expression information as the combination of the shared information (expression similarities) across different expressions and the unique information (expression-specific variations) for each expression. More specifically, FDRL mainly consists of two crucial networks: a Feature Decomposition Network (FDN) and a Feature Reconstruction Network (FRN). 37. Filter Response Normalization Layer: Eliminating Batch Dependence in the Training of Deep Neural Networks

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/1911.09737v2
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Batch Normalization (BN) uses mini-batch statistics to normalize the activations during training, introducing dependence between mini-batch elements. This dependency can hurt the performance if the mini-batch size is too small, or if the elements are correlated. Several alternatives, such as Batch Renormalization and Group Normalization (GN), have been proposed to address this issue. However, they either do not match the performance of BN for large batches, or still exhibit degradation in performance for smaller batches, or introduce artificial constraints on the model architecture. In this paper we propose the Filter Response Normalization (FRN) layer, a novel combination of a normalization and an activation function, that can be used as a replacement for other normalizations and activations. Our method operates on each activation channel of each batch element independently, eliminating the dependency on other batch elements. Our method outperforms BN and other alternatives in a variety of settings for all batch sizes. FRN layer performs $\approx 0.7-1.0\%$ better than BN on top-1 validation accuracy with large mini-batch sizes for Imagenet classification using InceptionV3 and Res
  • 易漏细节梳理：

BN的mini-batch统计会导致mini-batch元素之间的依赖性，这种依赖性可能会影响性能，尤其是在mini-batch太小或元素相关时。Batch Renormalization和Group Normalization等替代方案未能完全解决此问题。相比之下，FRN层独立地作用于每个激活通道的每个mini-batch元素，消除了与其他mini-batch元素的依赖性。因此，FRN层在各种设置中优于BN和其他替代方案，适用于所有mini-batch大小。具体而言，在大型mini-batch大小下，FRN层在ImageNet分类上的top-1验证准确率比BN高出约0.7-1.0%；在小型mini-batch大小下，FRN层比GN高出超过1%。此外，FRN层在COCO数据集上的目标检测问题上，比其他方法至少高出0.3-0.5%。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • BN的mini-batch统计会导致mini-batch元素之间的依赖性。
  • 这种依赖性可能会影响性能，尤其是在mini-batch太小或元素相关时。
  • Batch Renormalization和Group Normalization等替代方案未能完全解决此问题。
  • FRN层独立地作用于每个激活通道的每个mini-batch元素，消除了与其他mini-batch元素的依赖性。
  • FRN层在各种设置中优于BN和其他替代方案，适用于所有mini-batch大小。
  • FRN层在大型mini-batch大小下比BN在ImageNet分类上的top-1验证准确率高出约0.7-1.0%。
  • 在小型mini-batch大小下，FRN层比GN在相同问题上的表现高出超过1%。
  • FRN层在COCO数据集上的目标检测问题上，比其他方法至少高出0.3-0.5%。

[1911.09737v2] Filter Response Normalization Layer: Eliminating Batch Dependence in the Training of Deep Neural Networks Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:1911.09737v2 (cs) [Submitted on 21 Nov 2019 ( v1 ), last revised 1 Apr 2020 (this version, v2)] Title: Filter Response Normalization Layer: Eliminating Batch Dependence in the Training of Deep Neural Networks Authors: Saurabh Singh , Shankar Krishnan View a PDF of the paper titled Filter Response Normalization Layer: Eliminating Batch Dependence in the Training of Deep Neural Networks, by Saurabh Singh and 1 other authors View PDF Abstract: Batch Normalization (BN) uses mini-batch statistics to normalize the activations during training, introducing dependence between mini-batch elements. This dependency can hurt the performance if the mini-batch size is too small, or if the elements are correlated. Several alternatives, such as Batch Renormalization and Group Normalization (GN), have been proposed to address this issue. However, they either do not match the performance of BN for large batches, or still exhibit degradation in performance for smaller batches, or introduce artificial constraints on the model architecture. In this paper we propose the Filter Response Normalization (FRN) layer, a novel combination of a normalization and an activation function, that can be used as a replacement for other normalizations and activations. Our method operates on each activation channel of each batch element independently, eliminating the dependency on other batch elements. Our method outperforms BN and other alternatives in a variety of settings for all batch sizes. FRN layer performs $\approx 0.7-1.0\%$ better than BN on top-1 validation accuracy with large mini-batch sizes for Imagenet classification using InceptionV3 and ResnetV2-50 architectures. Further, it performs $>1\%$ better than GN on the same problem in the small mini-batch size regime. For object detection problem on COCO dataset, FRN layer outperforms all other methods by at least $0.3-0.5\%$ in all batch size regimes. 38. Multilevel Training for Kolmogorov Arnold Networks

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04827v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Algorithmic speedup of training common neural architectures is made difficult by the lack of structure guaranteed by the function compositions inherent to such networks. In contrast to multilayer perceptrons (MLPs), Kolmogorov-Arnold networks (KANs) provide more structure by expanding learned activations in a specified basis. This paper exploits this structure to develop practical algorithms and theoretical insights, yielding training speedup via multilevel training for KANs. To do so, we first establish an equivalence between KANs with spline basis functions and multichannel MLPs with power ReLU activations through a linear change of basis. We then analyze how this change of basis affects the geometry of gradient-based optimization with respect to spline knots. The KANs change-of-basis motivates a multilevel training approach, where we train a sequence of KANs naturally defined through a uniform refinement of spline knots with analytic geometric interpolation operators between models. The interpolation scheme enables a ``properly nested hierarchy'' of architectures, ensuring that interpolation to a fine model preserves the progress made on coarse models, while the compact support
  • 易漏细节梳理：

KANs的结构通过在指定基上展开激活函数获得，这一过程与多通道MLPs通过线性基变换等价。KANs的基变换不仅影响基于样条结点的梯度优化几何，还促使采用均匀细化样条结点的多级训练方法。样条基函数的紧支撑确保了后续级别的互补优化，从而使得精细模型能够保留粗糙模型的进展。因此，多级训练方法不仅能够显著提高训练性能，还能实现数量级的准确性提升。KANs的设计原则带来了可利用的结构，使得多级算法可以大幅提高训练表现。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • KANs的结构通过在指定基上展开激活函数获得。
  • KANs与多通道MLPs通过线性基变换等价。
  • KANs的基变换影响基于样条结点的梯度优化几何。
  • KANs的基变换促使采用均匀细化样条结点的多级训练方法。
  • 样条基函数的紧支撑确保了后续级别的互补优化。
  • 多级训练方法确保精细模型保留粗糙模型的进展。
  • 多级算法可以显著提高训练性能。
  • 多级训练方法能实现数量级的准确性提升。
  • KANs的设计原则可以带来可利用的结构。
  • 多级算法可以大幅提高训练表现。

[2603.04827v1] Multilevel Training for Kolmogorov Arnold Networks Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2603.04827v1 (cs) [Submitted on 5 Mar 2026] Title: Multilevel Training for Kolmogorov Arnold Networks Authors: Ben S. Southworth , Jonas A. Actor , Graham Harper , Eric C. Cyr View a PDF of the paper titled Multilevel Training for Kolmogorov Arnold Networks, by Ben S. Southworth and 3 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Algorithmic speedup of training common neural architectures is made difficult by the lack of structure guaranteed by the function compositions inherent to such networks. In contrast to multilayer perceptrons (MLPs), Kolmogorov-Arnold networks (KANs) provide more structure by expanding learned activations in a specified basis. This paper exploits this structure to develop practical algorithms and theoretical insights, yielding training speedup via multilevel training for KANs. To do so, we first establish an equivalence between KANs with spline basis functions and multichannel MLPs with power ReLU activations through a linear change of basis. We then analyze how this change of basis affects the geometry of gradient-based optimization with respect to spline knots. The KANs change-of-basis motivates a multilevel training approach, where we train a sequence of KANs naturally defined through a uniform refinement of spline knots with analytic geometric interpolation operators between models. The interpolation scheme enables a ``properly nested hierarchy'' of architectures, ensuring that interpolation to a fine model preserves the progress made on coarse models, while the compact support of spline basis functions ensures complementary optimization on subsequent levels. Numerical experiments demonstrate that our multilevel training approach can achieve orders of magnitude improvement in accuracy over conventional methods to train comparable KANs or MLPs, particularly for physics informed neural networks. Finally, this work demonstrates how principled design of neural networks can lead to exploitable structure, and in this case, multilevel algorithms that can dramatically improve training performance. 39. AgentSelect: Benchmark for Narrative Query-to-Agent Recommendation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03761v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：LLM agents are rapidly becoming the practical interface for task automation, yet the ecosystem lacks a principled way to choose among an exploding space of deployable configurations. Existing LLM leaderboards and tool/agent benchmarks evaluate components in isolation and remain fragmented across tasks, metrics, and candidate pools, leaving a critical research gap: there is little query-conditioned supervision for learning to recommend end-to-end agent configurations that couple a backbone model with a toolkit. We address this gap with AgentSelect, a benchmark that reframes agent selection as narrative query-to-agent recommendation over capability profiles and systematically converts heterogeneous evaluation artifacts into unified, positive-only interaction data. AgentSelectcomprises 111,179 queries, 107,721 deployable agents, and 251,103 interaction records aggregated from 40+ sources, spanning LLM-only, toolkit-only, and compositional agents. Our analyses reveal a regime shift from dense head reuse to long-tail, near one-off supervision, where popularity-based CF/GNN methods become fragile and content-aware capability matching is essential. We further show that Part~III synthesize
  • 易漏细节梳理：

query-conditioned监督对于学习端到端代理配置至关重要，这有助于提高代理性能。然而，评价代理时存在的碎片化问题，即不同任务和指标之间的评价碎片化，使得选择合适的代理变得困难。此外，基于流行度的方法在长尾、近于一次性监督场景中变得脆弱，这进一步加剧了选择代理的难度。因此，内容感知的能力匹配成为有效代理推荐的关键，它能够根据代理的内容和需求进行匹配，从而提高推荐的准确性。此外，可组合的交互学习能够覆盖更真实的交互组合，从而提高代理推荐的覆盖率。通过在AgentSelect上进行训练，模型能够顺利转移到公共代理市场，从而获得一致的性能提升。AgentSelect提供了一个统一的数据和评价基础设施，用于代理推荐，这为研究和加速新兴代理生态系统奠定了可重复的基础。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • query-conditioned supervision is crucial for learning end-to-end agent configurations.
  • fragmented evaluation artifacts across tasks and metrics hinder principled agent selection.
  • popularity-based methods become fragile in long-tail, near one-off supervision scenarios.
  • content-aware capability matching is essential for effective agent recommendation.
  • compositional interactions are learnable and improve coverage over realistic compositions.
  • models trained on AgentSelect transfer to a public agent marketplace, yielding consistent gains.
  • AgentSelect provides a unified data and evaluation infrastructure for agent recommendation.
  • reproducible foundation is established to study and accelerate the emerging agent ecosystem.

[2603.03761v1] AgentSelect: Benchmark for Narrative Query-to-Agent Recommendation Computer Science > Artificial Intelligence arXiv:2603.03761v1 (cs) [Submitted on 4 Mar 2026] Title: AgentSelect: Benchmark for Narrative Query-to-Agent Recommendation Authors: Yunxiao Shi , Wujiang Xu , Tingwei Chen , Haoning Shang , Ling Yang , Yunfeng Wan , Zhuo Cao , Xing Zi , Dimitris N. Metaxas , Min Xu View a PDF of the paper titled AgentSelect: Benchmark for Narrative Query-to-Agent Recommendation, by Yunxiao Shi and 9 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: LLM agents are rapidly becoming the practical interface for task automation, yet the ecosystem lacks a principled way to choose among an exploding space of deployable configurations. Existing LLM leaderboards and tool/agent benchmarks evaluate components in isolation and remain fragmented across tasks, metrics, and candidate pools, leaving a critical research gap: there is little query-conditioned supervision for learning to recommend end-to-end agent configurations that couple a backbone model with a toolkit. We address this gap with AgentSelect, a benchmark that reframes agent selection as narrative query-to-agent recommendation over capability profiles and systematically converts heterogeneous evaluation artifacts into unified, positive-only interaction data. AgentSelectcomprises 111,179 queries, 107,721 deployable agents, and 251,103 interaction records aggregated from 40+ sources, spanning LLM-only, toolkit-only, and compositional agents. Our analyses reveal a regime shift from dense head reuse to long-tail, near one-off supervision, where popularity-based CF/GNN methods become fragile and content-aware capability matching is essential. We further show that Part~III synthesized compositional interactions are learnable, induce capability-sensitive behavior under controlled counterfactual edits, and improve coverage over realistic compositions; models trained on AgentSelect also transfer to a public agent marketplace (MuleRun), yielding consistent gains on an unseen catalog. Overall, AgentSelect provides the first unified data and evaluation infrastructure for agent recommendation, which establishes a reproducible foundation to study and accelerate the emerging agent ecosystem. 40. Learning multi-domain feature relation for visible and Long-wave Infrared image patch matching

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2308.04880v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Recently, learning-based algorithms have achieved promising performance on cross-spectral image patch matching, which, however, is still far from satisfactory for practical application. On the one hand, a lack of large-scale dataset with diverse scenes haunts its further improvement for learning-based algorithms, whose performances and generalization rely heavily on the dataset size and diversity. On the other hand, more emphasis has been put on feature relation in the spatial domain whereas the scale dependency between features has often been ignored, leading to performance degeneration especially when encountering significant appearance variations for cross-spectral patches. To address these issues, we publish, to be best of our knowledge, the largest visible and Long-wave Infrared (LWIR) image patch matching dataset, termed VL-CMIM, which contains 1300 pairs of strictly aligned visible and LWIR images and over 2 million patch pairs covering diverse scenes such as asteroid, field, country, build, street and water.In addition, a multi-domain feature relation learning network (MD-FRN) is proposed. Input by the features extracted from a four-branch network, both feature relations in
  • 易漏细节梳理：

学习算法依赖于大规模多样化的数据集，否则性能和泛化能力会受限。VL-CMIM 数据集作为目前最大的可见光和长波红外图像匹配数据集，为跨光谱图像匹配提供了丰富多样的样本。然而，忽视特征在尺度上的依赖关系会导致性能下降，尤其是在跨光谱图像匹配时遇到显著外观变化。MD-FRN 网络通过学习空间和尺度特征关系来提高跨光谱图像匹配的性能，但尺度依赖性在特征关系学习中经常被忽略，这进一步导致了性能的下降。因此，通过多域特征关系学习网络可以进一步聚合多域关系，提高模型的鲁棒性。此外，交换学习到的空间关系和尺度关系特征可以增强模型的跨域特征关系学习能力，从而提升整体性能。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 学习算法依赖于大规模多样化的数据集，否则性能和泛化能力会受限。
  • 忽视特征在尺度上的依赖关系会导致性能下降，尤其是在跨光谱图像匹配时遇到显著外观变化。
  • VL-CMIM 数据集是目前最大的可见光和长波红外图像匹配数据集。
  • MD-FRN 网络通过学习空间和尺度特征关系来提高跨光谱图像匹配的性能。
  • 尺度依赖性在特征关系学习中经常被忽略，这会导致性能下降。
  • 通过多域特征关系学习网络可以进一步聚合多域关系，提高模型的鲁棒性。
  • 交换学习到的空间关系和尺度关系特征可以增强模型的跨域特征关系学习能力。

[2308.04880v1] Learning multi-domain feature relation for visible and Long-wave Infrared image patch matching Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2308.04880v1 (cs) [Submitted on 9 Aug 2023] Title: Learning multi-domain feature relation for visible and Long-wave Infrared image patch matching Authors: Xiuwei Zhang , Yanping Li , Zhaoshuai Qi , Yi Sun , Yanning Zhang View a PDF of the paper titled Learning multi-domain feature relation for visible and Long-wave Infrared image patch matching, by Xiuwei Zhang and 4 other authors View PDF Abstract: Recently, learning-based algorithms have achieved promising performance on cross-spectral image patch matching, which, however, is still far from satisfactory for practical application. On the one hand, a lack of large-scale dataset with diverse scenes haunts its further improvement for learning-based algorithms, whose performances and generalization rely heavily on the dataset size and diversity. On the other hand, more emphasis has been put on feature relation in the spatial domain whereas the scale dependency between features has often been ignored, leading to performance degeneration especially when encountering significant appearance variations for cross-spectral patches. To address these issues, we publish, to be best of our knowledge, the largest visible and Long-wave Infrared (LWIR) image patch matching dataset, termed VL-CMIM, which contains 1300 pairs of strictly aligned visible and LWIR images and over 2 million patch pairs covering diverse scenes such as asteroid, field, country, build, street and this http URL addition, a multi-domain feature relation learning network (MD-FRN) is proposed. Input by the features extracted from a four-branch network, both feature relations in spatial and scale domains are learned via a spatial correlation module (SCM) and multi-scale adaptive aggregation module (MSAG), respectively. To further aggregate the multi-domain relations, a deep domain interactive mechanism (DIM) is applied, where the learnt spatial-relation and scale-relation features are exchanged and further input into MSCRM and SCM. This mechanism allows our model to learn interactive cross-domain feature relations, leading to improved robustness to significant appearance changes due to different modality. 41. Bi-directional Feature Reconstruction Network for Fine-Grained Few-Shot Image Classification

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2211.17161v2
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The main challenge for fine-grained few-shot image classification is to learn feature representations with higher inter-class and lower intra-class variations, with a mere few labelled samples. Conventional few-shot learning methods however cannot be naively adopted for this fine-grained setting -- a quick pilot study reveals that they in fact push for the opposite (i.e., lower inter-class variations and higher intra-class variations). To alleviate this problem, prior works predominately use a support set to reconstruct the query image and then utilize metric learning to determine its category. Upon careful inspection, we further reveal that such unidirectional reconstruction methods only help to increase inter-class variations and are not effective in tackling intra-class variations. In this paper, we for the first time introduce a bi-reconstruction mechanism that can simultaneously accommodate for inter-class and intra-class variations. In addition to using the support set to reconstruct the query set for increasing inter-class variations, we further use the query set to reconstruct the support set for reducing intra-class variations. This design effectively helps the model to ex
  • 易漏细节梳理：

fine-grained few-shot学习要求特征表示具有高类间差异和低类内差异，但传统few-shot学习方法难以直接应用于细粒度分类场景。为解决这一问题，研究引入了双向重建机制，该机制能够同时处理类间和类内差异。具体而言，单向重建方法仅能增加类间差异，而无法解决类内差异问题，因此需要进一步改进。通过查询集对支持集进行重建，可以有效减少类内差异，从而增强特征的区分性。此外，自重建模块进一步增强了这一效果，使得特征更加区分性。实验结果表明，这种双向机制和自重建模块共同作用的方法在多个细粒度图像分类数据集上表现优异，证明了其有效性和优越性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • fine-grained few-shot学习需要高类间差异和低类内差异的特征表示。
  • 传统few-shot学习方法不能直接应用于细粒度分类场景。
  • 单向重建方法只能增加类间差异，不能解决类内差异问题。
  • 双向重建机制可以同时处理类间和类内差异。
  • 查询集可以用于重建支持集，以减少类内差异。
  • 自重建模块可以进一步增强特征的区分性。
  • 实验结果表明，该方法在多个细粒度图像分类数据集上表现优异。
  • 双向机制和自重建模块共同工作，使特征更加区分性。

[2211.17161v2] Bi-directional Feature Reconstruction Network for Fine-Grained Few-Shot Image Classification Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2211.17161v2 (cs) [Submitted on 30 Nov 2022 ( v1 ), last revised 9 Jan 2023 (this version, v2)] Title: Bi-directional Feature Reconstruction Network for Fine-Grained Few-Shot Image Classification Authors: Jijie Wu , Dongliang Chang , Aneeshan Sain , Xiaoxu Li , Zhanyu Ma , Jie Cao , Jun Guo , Yi-Zhe Song View a PDF of the paper titled Bi-directional Feature Reconstruction Network for Fine-Grained Few-Shot Image Classification, by Jijie Wu and 7 other authors View PDF Abstract: The main challenge for fine-grained few-shot image classification is to learn feature representations with higher inter-class and lower intra-class variations, with a mere few labelled samples. Conventional few-shot learning methods however cannot be naively adopted for this fine-grained setting -- a quick pilot study reveals that they in fact push for the opposite (i.e., lower inter-class variations and higher intra-class variations). To alleviate this problem, prior works predominately use a support set to reconstruct the query image and then utilize metric learning to determine its category. Upon careful inspection, we further reveal that such unidirectional reconstruction methods only help to increase inter-class variations and are not effective in tackling intra-class variations. In this paper, we for the first time introduce a bi-reconstruction mechanism that can simultaneously accommodate for inter-class and intra-class variations. In addition to using the support set to reconstruct the query set for increasing inter-class variations, we further use the query set to reconstruct the support set for reducing intra-class variations. This design effectively helps the model to explore more subtle and discriminative features which is key for the fine-grained problem in hand. Furthermore, we also construct a self-reconstruction module to work alongside the bi-directional module to make the features even more discriminative. Experimental results on three widely used fine-grained image classification datasets consistently show considerable improvements compared with other methods. Codes are available at: this https URL . 42. Online Realizable Regression and Applications for ReLU Networks

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.19172v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Realizable online regression can behave very differently from online classification. Even without any margin or stochastic assumptions, realizability may enforce horizon-free (finite) cumulative loss under metric-like losses, even when the analogous classification problem has an infinite mistake bound. We study realizable online regression in the adversarial model under losses that satisfy an approximate triangle inequality (approximate pseudo-metrics). Recent work of Attias et al. shows that the minimax realizable cumulative loss is characterized by the scaled Littlestone/online dimension $\mathbb{D}{\mathrm{onl}}$, but this quantity can be difficult to analyze. Our main contribution is a generic potential method that upper bounds $\mathbb{D}}$ by a concrete Dudley-type entropy integral that depends only on covering numbers of the hypothesis class under the induced sup pseudo-metric. We define an \emph{entropy potential} $Φ(\mathcal{H})=\int_{0}^{diam(\mathcal{H})} \log N(\mathcal{H},\varepsilon)\,d\varepsilon$, where $N(\mathcal{H},\varepsilon)$ is the $\varepsilon$-covering number of $\mathcal{H}$, and show that for every $c$-approximate pseudo-metric loss, $\ma
  • 易漏细节梳理：

易漏但重要的概念包括：首先，无视野累积损失可以是有限的，即使分类问题的错误边界是无限的。其次，近似伪度量损失满足近似的三角不等式。此外，缩放的Littlestone/在线维度$\mathbb{D}_{\mathrm{onl}}$可以表征最小最大可实现累积损失，但分析起来较为困难。因此，熵潜力$\Phi(\mathcal{H})$依赖于假设类的覆盖数，而有界范数$k$-ReLU网络可以实现有限的回归损失，甚至$\widetilde O(k^2)$，对于一个ReLU则为$O(1)$。然而，对于$k=2,d=1$，有界范数$k$-ReLU网络无法实现分类。因此，可实现的在线学习和回归问题可能与分类问题表现出不同的行为。此外，最小最大可实现累积损失由缩放的Littlestone/在线维度$\mathbb{D}_{\mathrm{onl}}$表征，而熵潜力$\Phi(\mathcal{H})$提供了对有效维度的透明依赖性。覆盖数在假设类下诱导的sup伪度量中至关重要，用于分析$\mathbb{D}_{\mathrm{onl}}$。因此，通过多项式度量熵可以实现无视野可实现累积损失。最后，有界范数$k$-ReLU网络在回归和分类之间存在明显的二分法，而可实现的在线学习和回归问题在满足一定条件时可以高效解决。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • horizon-free cumulative loss can be finite even when the classification problem has an infinite mistake bound.
  • approximate pseudo-metric losses satisfy an approximate triangle inequality.
  • scaled Littlestone/online dimension $\mathbb{D}_{\mathrm{onl}}$ characterizes minimax realizable cumulative loss but can be hard to analyze.
  • entropy potential $\Phi(\mathcal{H})$ depends on covering numbers of the hypothesis class.
  • polynomial metric entropy implies a finite horizon-free realizable cumulative-loss bound.
  • finite and efficiently achievable total loss for $L$-Lipschitz regression is possible if $q>d$, otherwise infinite.
  • bounded-norm $k$-ReLU networks can achieve finite regression loss, even $\widetilde O(k^2)$, and $O(1)$ for one ReLU.
  • classification with $k=2,d=1$ is impossible for bounded-norm $k$-ReLU networks.
  • realizable online learning and regression problems can have different behaviors compared to classification problems.
  • minimax realizable cumulative loss is characterized by the scaled Littlestone/online dimension $\mathbb{D}_{\mathrm{onl}}$.
  • entropy potential $\Phi(\mathcal{H})$ provides a transparent dependence on effective dimension.
  • covering numbers of the hypothesis class under the induced sup pseudo-metric are crucial for analyzing $\mathbb{D}_{\mathrm{onl}}$.
  • horizon-free realizable cumulative-loss bounds can be achieved with polynomial metric entropy.
  • dichotomy between regression and classification for bounded-norm $k$-ReLU networks is sharp.
  • realizable online learning and regression problems can be efficiently solved under certain conditions.

[2602.19172v1] Online Realizable Regression and Applications for ReLU Networks Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2602.19172v1 (cs) [Submitted on 22 Feb 2026] Title: Online Realizable Regression and Applications for ReLU Networks Authors: Ilan Doron-Arad , Idan Mehalel , Elchanan Mossel View a PDF of the paper titled Online Realizable Regression and Applications for ReLU Networks, by Ilan Doron-Arad and Idan Mehalel and Elchanan Mossel View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Realizable online regression can behave very differently from online classification. Even without any margin or stochastic assumptions, realizability may enforce horizon-free (finite) cumulative loss under metric-like losses, even when the analogous classification problem has an infinite mistake bound. We study realizable online regression in the adversarial model under losses that satisfy an approximate triangle inequality (approximate pseudo-metrics). Recent work of Attias et al. shows that the minimax realizable cumulative loss is characterized by the scaled Littlestone/online dimension $\mathbb{D}{\mathrm{onl}}$, but this quantity can be difficult to analyze. Our main contribution is a generic potential method that upper bounds $\mathbb{D}}$ by a concrete Dudley-type entropy integral that depends only on covering numbers of the hypothesis class under the induced sup pseudo-metric. We define an \emph{entropy potential} $\Phi(\mathcal{H})=\int_{0}^{diam(\mathcal{H})} \log N(\mathcal{H},\varepsilon)\,d\varepsilon$, where $N(\mathcal{H},\varepsilon)$ is the $\varepsilon$-covering number of $\mathcal{H}$, and show that for every $c$-approximate pseudo-metric loss, $\mathbb{D}{\mathrm{onl}}(\mathcal{H})\le O(c)\,\Phi(\mathcal{H})$. In particular, polynomial metric entropy implies $\Phi(\mathcal{H})<\infty$ and hence a horizon-free realizable cumulative-loss bound with transparent dependence on effective dimension. We illustrate the method on two families. We prove a sharp $q$-vs.-$d$ dichotomy for realizable online learning (finite and efficiently achievable $\Theta(L^d)$ total loss for $L$-Lipschitz regression iff $q>d$, otherwise infinite), and for bounded-norm $k$-ReLU networks separate regression (finite loss, even $\widetilde O(k^2)$, and $O(1)$ for one ReLU) from classification (impossible already for $k=2,d=1$). 43. Recovering Faces from Portraits with Auxiliary Facial Attributes

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/1904.03612v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Recovering a photorealistic face from an artistic portrait is a challenging task since crucial facial details are often distorted or completely lost in artistic compositions. To handle this loss, we propose an Attribute-guided Face Recovery from Portraits (AFRP) that utilizes a Face Recovery Network (FRN) and a Discriminative Network (DN). FRN consists of an autoencoder with residual block-embedded skip-connections and incorporates facial attribute vectors into the feature maps of input portraits at the bottleneck of the autoencoder. DN has multiple convolutional and fully-connected layers, and its role is to enforce FRN to generate authentic face images with corresponding facial attributes dictated by the input attribute vectors. %Leveraging on the spatial transformer networks, FRN automatically compensates for misalignments of portraits. % and generates aligned face images. For the preservation of identities, we impose the recovered and ground-truth faces to share similar visual features. Specifically, DN determines whether the recovered image looks like a real face and checks if the facial attributes extracted from the recovered image are consistent with given attributes. %Our m
  • 易漏细节梳理：

AFRP（高级面部恢复网络）利用特征图中的面部属性向量来恢复高质量的逼真面部图像，而FRN（面部恢复网络）中的残差块嵌入了跳连连接，有助于进一步恢复面部特征。DN（鉴别网络）通过检查恢复图像的面部属性是否与输入属性向量一致，确保生成真实且保持身份的面部图像。因此，恢复的面部图像和真实面部图像应具有相似的视觉特征，以保持身份。AFRP不仅能够从未对齐的肖像中恢复高质量的逼真面部图像，还能从未见过的风格化肖像、艺术画作和手绘草图中恢复逼真且保持身份的面部图像。在大规模合成和草图数据集上，AFRP达到了最先进的结果，能够恢复具有所需属性的逼真且保持身份的面部图像。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • AFRP利用了特征图中的面部属性向量来恢复面部细节。
  • FRN中的残差块嵌入了跳连连接，有助于恢复面部特征。
  • DN通过检查恢复图像的面部属性是否与输入属性向量一致来确保生成真实面部图像。
  • AFRP能够从未对齐的肖像中恢复高质量的逼真面部图像。
  • DN通过检查恢复图像是否看起来像真实面部图像来确保生成真实面部图像。
  • 恢复的面部图像和真实面部图像应具有相似的视觉特征以保持身份。
  • AFRP能够从未见过的风格化肖像、艺术画作和手绘草图中恢复逼真且保持身份的面部图像。
  • 在大规模合成和草图数据集上，AFRP达到了最先进的结果。
  • AFRP可以恢复具有所需属性的逼真且保持身份的面部图像。

Specifically, DN determines whether the recovered image looks like a real face and checks if the facial attributes extracted from the recovered image are consistent with given attributes. %Our method can recover high-quality photorealistic faces from unaligned portraits while preserving the identity of the face images as well as it can reconstruct a photorealistic face image with a desired set of attributes. Our method can recover photorealistic identity-preserving faces with desired attributes from unseen stylized portraits, artistic paintings, and hand-drawn sketches. On large-scale synthesized and sketch datasets, we demonstrate that our face recovery method achieves state-of-the-art results. 44. Adaptive Sampling for Storage of Progressive Images on DNA

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05220v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The short lifespan of traditional data storage media, coupled with an exponential increase in storage demand, has made long-term archival a fundamental problem in the data storage industry and beyond. Consequently, researchers are looking for innovative media solutions that can store data over long time periods at a very low cost. DNA molecules, with their high density, long lifespan, and low energy needs, have emerged as a viable alternative to digital data archival. However, current DNA data storage technologies are facing challenges with respect to cost and reliability. Thus, coding rate and error robustness are critical to scale DNA storage and make it technologically and economically achievable. Moreover, the molecules of DNA that encode different files are often located in the same oligo pool. Without random access solutions at the oligo level, it is very impractical to decode a specific file from these mixed pools, as all oligos need to first be sequenced and decoded before a target file can be retrieved, which greatly deteriorates the read cost. This paper introduces a solution to efficiently encode and store images into DNA molecules, that aims at reducing the read cost
  • 易漏细节梳理：

传统存储介质的寿命短使得长期存档成为难题，而DNA存储技术作为一种新兴的存储方式，虽然具有潜在的巨大存储容量和长久保存的优势，但当前仍面临成本高昂和可靠性不足的挑战。为了提高DNA存储技术的性能，关键在于提升编码率和增强错误鲁棒性。然而，在同一个寡核苷酸池中存储不同文件会增加读取成本，因此，适应性采样方法被引入，通过调整要读取的分辨率，可以在测序时选择特定的寡核苷酸，从而提供了一种PCR-free的随机访问解决方案。此外，JPEG2000的渐进解码功能也被应用于图像存储系统，进一步优化了读取过程，降低了成本。因此，通过这些技术手段，DNA存储技术在克服现有挑战的同时，逐渐展现出其在长期存档领域的巨大潜力。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 传统存储介质的寿命短导致长期存档成为难题。
  • DNA存储技术的成本和可靠性是当前面临的主要挑战。
  • 编码率和错误鲁棒性是提高DNA存储技术的关键。
  • 在同一个寡核苷酸池中存储不同文件会导致读取成本增加。
  • JPEG2000的渐进解码功能被用于图像存储系统。
  • 适应性采样方法可以调整要读取的分辨率。
  • 适应性采样方法可以在测序时选择特定的寡核苷酸。
  • 这种方法提供了一种PCR-free的随机访问解决方案。

[2603.05220v1] Adaptive Sampling for Storage of Progressive Images on DNA Electrical Engineering and Systems Science > Image and Video Processing arXiv:2603.05220v1 (eess) [Submitted on 5 Mar 2026] Title: Adaptive Sampling for Storage of Progressive Images on DNA Authors: Xavier Pic , Nimesh Pinnamaneni , Raja Appuswamy View a PDF of the paper titled Adaptive Sampling for Storage of Progressive Images on DNA, by Xavier Pic and Nimesh Pinnamaneni and Raja Appuswamy View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: The short lifespan of traditional data storage media, coupled with an exponential increase in storage demand, has made long-term archival a fundamental problem in the data storage industry and beyond. Consequently, researchers are looking for innovative media solutions that can store data over long time periods at a very low cost. DNA molecules, with their high density, long lifespan, and low energy needs, have emerged as a viable alternative to digital data archival. However, current DNA data storage technologies are facing challenges with respect to cost and reliability. Thus, coding rate and error robustness are critical to scale DNA storage and make it technologically and economically achievable. Moreover, the molecules of DNA that encode different files are often located in the same oligo pool. Without random access solutions at the oligo level, it is very impractical to decode a specific file from these mixed pools, as all oligos need to first be sequenced and decoded before a target file can be retrieved, which greatly deteriorates the read cost. This paper introduces a solution to efficiently encode and store images into DNA molecules, that aims at reducing the read cost necessary to retrieve a resolution-reduced version of an image. This image storage system is based on the Progressive Decoding Functionality of the JPEG2000 codec but can be adapted to any conventional progressive codec. Each resolution layer is encoded into a set of oligos using the JPEG DNA VM codec, a DNA-based coder that aims at retrieving a file with a high reliability. Depending on the desired resolution to be read, the set of oligos as well as the portion of the oligos to be sequenced and decoded are adjusted accordingly. These oligos will be selected at sequencing time, with the help of the adaptive sampling method provided by the Nanopore sequencers, making it a PCR-free random access solution. 45. Quantitative Convergence of Wasserstein Gradient Flows of Kernel Mean Discrepancies

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.01977v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We study the quantitative convergence of Wasserstein gradient flows of Kernel Mean Discrepancy (KMD) (also known as Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD)) functionals. Our setting covers in particular the training dynamics of shallow neural networks in the infinite-width and continuous time limit, as well as interacting particle systems with pairwise Riesz kernel interaction in the mean-field and overdamped limit. Our main analysis concerns the model case of KMD functionals given by the squared Sobolev distance $ \mathscr{E}^ν_{s}(μ)= \frac{1}{2}\lVert μ-ν\rVert_{\dot H^{-s}}^{2}$ for any $s\geq 1 $ and $ν$ a fixed probability measure on the $d$-dimensional torus. First, inspired by Yudovich theory for the $2d$-Euler equation, we establish existence and uniqueness in natural weak regularity classes. Next, we show that for $s=1$ the flow converges globally at an exponential rate under minimal assumptions, while for $s>1$ we prove local convergence at polynomial rates that depend explicitly on $s$ and on the Sobolev regularity of $μ$ and $ν$. These rates hold both at the energy level and in higher regularity classes and are tight for $ν$ uniform. We then consider the gradient flow of the po
  • 易漏细节梳理：

Wasserstein梯度流可以用于KMD函数的全局收敛，对于\(s=1\)的情况，这种收敛可以以指数速率进行。而对于\(s>1\)的情况，收敛速率则为多项式，并且依赖于\(s\)和Sobolev正则性。这种分析适用于在无限宽度和连续时间极限下的浅层神经网络。此外，这些收敛速率不仅在能量水平上成立，还在更高正则性类中有效。特别地，当\(s=1\)时，这一情况在所有设置中之前都是非量化收敛的，因此是一个开放问题。浅层神经网络使用ReLU激活时的动态可以被描述为Wasserstein--Fisher--Rao梯度流。通过与Sobolev能量情况的对应，可以明确地推导出多项式收敛速率。此外，这种分析还通过数值实验在维度\(d=1\)中得到了验证，使用了PDE和粒子方法两种方法。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • Wasserstein gradient flows of KMD functionals can converge globally at an exponential rate for \(s=1\).
  • For \(s>1\), convergence rates are polynomial and depend on \(s\) and Sobolev regularity.
  • The analysis applies to shallow neural networks in the infinite-width and continuous time limit.
  • The rates of convergence hold both at the energy level and in higher regularity classes.
  • The special case \(s=1\) was previously open for non-quantitative convergence in all settings.
  • The dynamics for shallow neural networks with ReLU activation can be cast as a Wasserstein--Fisher--Rao gradient flow.
  • A correspondence with the Sobolev energy case allows derivation of explicit polynomial convergence rates.
  • The analysis includes numerical experiments in dimension \(d=1\) using both PDE and particle methods.

[2603.01977v1] Quantitative Convergence of Wasserstein Gradient Flows of Kernel Mean Discrepancies Mathematics > Analysis of PDEs arXiv:2603.01977v1 (math) [Submitted on 2 Mar 2026] Title: Quantitative Convergence of Wasserstein Gradient Flows of Kernel Mean Discrepancies Authors: Lénaïc Chizat , Maria Colombo , Roberto Colombo , Xavier Fernández-Real View a PDF of the paper titled Quantitative Convergence of Wasserstein Gradient Flows of Kernel Mean Discrepancies, by L\'ena\"ic Chizat and 3 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: We study the quantitative convergence of Wasserstein gradient flows of Kernel Mean Discrepancy (KMD) (also known as Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD)) functionals. Our setting covers in particular the training dynamics of shallow neural networks in the infinite-width and continuous time limit, as well as interacting particle systems with pairwise Riesz kernel interaction in the mean-field and overdamped limit. Our main analysis concerns the model case of KMD functionals given by the squared Sobolev distance $ \mathscr{E}^{\nu}{s}(\mu)= \frac{1}{2}\lVert \mu-\nu\rVert}^{2}$ for any $s\geq 1 $ and $\nu$ a fixed probability measure on the $d$-dimensional torus. First, inspired by Yudovich theory for the $2d$-Euler equation, we establish existence and uniqueness in natural weak regularity classes. Next, we show that for $s=1$ the flow converges globally at an exponential rate under minimal assumptions, while for $s>1$ we prove local convergence at polynomial rates that depend explicitly on $s$ and on the Sobolev regularity of $\mu$ and $\nu$. These rates hold both at the energy level and in higher regularity classes and are tight for $\nu$ uniform. We then consider the gradient flow of the population loss for shallow neural networks with ReLU activation, which can be cast as a Wasserstein--Fisher--Rao gradient flow on the space of nonnegative measures on the sphere $\mathbb{S}^d$. Exploiting a correspondence with the Sobolev energy case with $s=(d+3)/2$, we derive an explicit polynomial local convergence rate for this dynamics. Except for the special case $s=1$, even non-quantitative convergence was previously open in all these settings. We also include numerical experiments in dimension $d=1$ using both PDE and particle methods which illustrate our analysis. 46. Learning to Compress Videos without Computing Motion

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2009.14110v3
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：With the development of higher resolution contents and displays, its significant volume poses significant challenges to the goals of acquiring, transmitting, compressing, and displaying high-quality video content. In this paper, we propose a new deep learning video compression architecture that does not require motion estimation, which is the most expensive element of modern hybrid video compression codecs like H.264 and HEVC. Our framework exploits the regularities inherent to video motion, which we capture by using displaced frame differences as video representations to train the neural network. In addition, we propose a new space-time reconstruction network based on both an LSTM model and a UNet model, which we call LSTM-UNet. The new video compression framework has three components: a Displacement Calculation Unit (DCU), a Displacement Compression Network (DCN), and a Frame Reconstruction Network (FRN). The DCU removes the need for motion estimation found in hybrid codecs and is less expensive. In the DCN, an RNN-based network is utilized to compress displaced frame differences as well as retain temporal information between frames. The LSTM-UNet is used in the FRN to learn spac
  • 易漏细节梳理：

现代混合视频压缩编解码器如H.264和HEVC中最昂贵的元素是运动估计，因此去除运动估计使得新的视频压缩框架更经济。为了实现这一目标，RNN网络被用于压缩移位帧差并保留帧间的时间信息，而LSTM-UNet则用于学习视频的空间-时间微分表示。实验结果表明，MOVI-Codec在MS-SSIM指标上优于H.264和HEVC，且无需进行运动估计。进一步地，LSTM-UNet在帧重建网络中用于学习空间-时间微分表示，使得新的视频压缩框架在高分辨率视频上优于H.266（VVC）。此外，Displacement Calculation Unit（DCU）的引入减少了对运动估计的需求，进一步增强了新框架的经济性和效率。因此，新的视频压缩框架不仅简化了处理流程，还显著提高了视频质量。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 现代混合视频压缩编解码器如H.264和HEVC中最昂贵的元素是运动估计。
  • 运动估计的去除使得新的视频压缩框架更经济。
  • RNN网络用于压缩移位帧差并保留帧间的时间信息。
  • LSTM-UNet用于学习视频的空间-时间微分表示。
  • 实验表明，MOVI-Codec在MS-SSIM指标上优于H.264和HEVC。
  • 新的视频压缩框架无需进行运动估计。
  • LSTM-UNet在帧重建网络中用于学习空间-时间微分表示。
  • 实验结果表明，MOVI-Codec在高分辨率视频上优于H.266（VVC）。
  • Displacement Calculation Unit（DCU）减少了对运动估计的需求。

[2009.14110v3] Learning to Compress Videos without Computing Motion Electrical Engineering and Systems Science > Image and Video Processing arXiv:2009.14110v3 (eess) [Submitted on 29 Sep 2020 ( v1 ), last revised 27 Mar 2022 (this version, v3)] Title: Learning to Compress Videos without Computing Motion Authors: Meixu Chen , Todd Goodall , Anjul Patney , Alan C. Bovik View a PDF of the paper titled Learning to Compress Videos without Computing Motion, by Meixu Chen and 3 other authors View PDF Abstract: With the development of higher resolution contents and displays, its significant volume poses significant challenges to the goals of acquiring, transmitting, compressing, and displaying high-quality video content. In this paper, we propose a new deep learning video compression architecture that does not require motion estimation, which is the most expensive element of modern hybrid video compression codecs like H.264 and HEVC. Our framework exploits the regularities inherent to video motion, which we capture by using displaced frame differences as video representations to train the neural network. In addition, we propose a new space-time reconstruction network based on both an LSTM model and a UNet model, which we call LSTM-UNet. The new video compression framework has three components: a Displacement Calculation Unit (DCU), a Displacement Compression Network (DCN), and a Frame Reconstruction Network (FRN). The DCU removes the need for motion estimation found in hybrid codecs and is less expensive. In the DCN, an RNN-based network is utilized to compress displaced frame differences as well as retain temporal information between frames. The LSTM-UNet is used in the FRN to learn space-time differential representations of videos. Our experimental results show that our compression model, which we call the MOtionless VIdeo Codec (MOVI-Codec), learns how to efficiently compress videos without computing motion. Our experiments show that MOVI-Codec outperforms the Low-Delay P veryfast setting of the video coding standard H.264 and exceeds the performance of the modern global standard HEVC codec, using the same setting, as measured by MS-SSIM, especially on higher resolution videos. In addition, our network outperforms the latest H.266 (VVC) codec at higher bitrates, when assessed using MS-SSIM, on high-resolution videos. 47. Orbital Transformers for Predicting Wavefunctions in Time-Dependent Density Functional Theory

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03511v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We aim to learn wavefunctions simulated by time-dependent density functional theory (TDDFT), which can be efficiently represented as linear combination coefficients of atomic orbitals. In real-time TDDFT, the electronic wavefunctions of a molecule evolve over time in response to an external excitation, enabling first-principles predictions of physical properties such as optical absorption, electron dynamics, and high-order response. However, conventional real-time TDDFT relies on time-consuming propagation of all occupied states with fine time steps. In this work, we propose OrbEvo, which is based on an equivariant graph transformer architecture and learns to evolve the full electronic wavefunction coefficients across time steps. First, to account for external field, we design an equivariant conditioning to encode both strength and direction of external electric field and break the symmetry from SO(3) to SO(2). Furthermore, we design two OrbEvo models, OrbEvo-WF and OrbEvo-DM, using wavefunction pooling and density matrix as interaction method, respectively. Motivated by the central role of the density functional in TDDFT, OrbEvo-DM encodes the density matrix aggregated from all oc
  • 易漏细节梳理：

OrbEvo模型通过学习原子轨道线性组合系数来预测波函数，而OrbEvo-WF模型和OrbEvo-DM模型则分别使用波函数池化和密度矩阵作为交互方法。其中，密度矩阵在时间依赖密度泛函理论（TDDFT）中扮演着核心角色，而OrbEvo-DM模型通过使用密度矩阵，能够更准确地捕捉在外场作用下的激发态量子动力学。为了限制时间依赖波函数的误差累积，训练策略被设计出来。此外，外部电场的强度和方向需要被编码以打破旋转对称性，从而提高模型的预测精度。生成的TDDFT数据集包括5000种不同分子和1500种分子配置，这些数据集使得OrbEvo模型能够准确预测时间依赖波函数、时间依赖偶极矩和光学吸收光谱。因此，OrbEvo模型在处理在外场作用下的激发态量子动力学方面表现出色，为相关研究提供了有力支持。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • OrbEvo模型通过学习原子轨道线性组合系数来预测波函数。
  • 外部电场的强度和方向需要被编码以打破旋转对称性。
  • OrbEvo-WF模型使用波函数池化作为交互方法。
  • OrbEvo-DM模型使用密度矩阵作为交互方法。
  • 密度矩阵在TDDFT中起着核心作用。
  • 训练策略旨在限制时间依赖波函数的误差累积。
  • 生成的TDDFT数据集包括5000种不同分子和1500种分子配置。
  • OrbEvo模型准确捕捉了在外场作用下的激发态量子动力学。
  • 时间依赖波函数、时间依赖偶极矩和光学吸收光谱被准确预测。

[2603.03511v1] Orbital Transformers for Predicting Wavefunctions in Time-Dependent Density Functional Theory Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2603.03511v1 (cs) [Submitted on 3 Mar 2026] Title: Orbital Transformers for Predicting Wavefunctions in Time-Dependent Density Functional Theory Authors: Xuan Zhang , Haiyang Yu , Chengdong Wang , Jacob Helwig , Shuiwang Ji , Xiaofeng Qian View a PDF of the paper titled Orbital Transformers for Predicting Wavefunctions in Time-Dependent Density Functional Theory, by Xuan Zhang and 5 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: We aim to learn wavefunctions simulated by time-dependent density functional theory (TDDFT), which can be efficiently represented as linear combination coefficients of atomic orbitals. In real-time TDDFT, the electronic wavefunctions of a molecule evolve over time in response to an external excitation, enabling first-principles predictions of physical properties such as optical absorption, electron dynamics, and high-order response. However, conventional real-time TDDFT relies on time-consuming propagation of all occupied states with fine time steps. In this work, we propose OrbEvo, which is based on an equivariant graph transformer architecture and learns to evolve the full electronic wavefunction coefficients across time steps. First, to account for external field, we design an equivariant conditioning to encode both strength and direction of external electric field and break the symmetry from SO(3) to SO(2). Furthermore, we design two OrbEvo models, OrbEvo-WF and OrbEvo-DM, using wavefunction pooling and density matrix as interaction method, respectively. Motivated by the central role of the density functional in TDDFT, OrbEvo-DM encodes the density matrix aggregated from all occupied electronic states into feature vectors via tensor contraction, providing a more intuitive approach to learn the time evolution operator. We adopt a training strategy specifically tailored to limit the error accumulation of time-dependent wavefunctions over autoregressive rollout. To evaluate our approach, we generate TDDFT datasets consisting of 5,000 different molecules in the QM9 dataset and 1,500 molecular configurations of the malonaldehyde molecule in the MD17 dataset. Results show that our OrbEvo model accurately captures quantum dynamics of excited states under external field, including time-dependent wavefunctions, time-dependent dipole moment, and optical absorption spectra. 48. Leveraging Model Soups to Classify Intangible Cultural Heritage Images from the Mekong Delta

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02181v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The classification of Intangible Cultural Heritage (ICH) images in the Mekong Delta poses unique challenges due to limited annotated data, high visual similarity among classes, and domain heterogeneity. In such low-resource settings, conventional deep learning models often suffer from high variance or overfit to spurious correlations, leading to poor generalization. To address these limitations, we propose a robust framework that integrates the hybrid CoAtNet architecture with model soups, a lightweight weight-space ensembling technique that averages checkpoints from a single training trajectory without increasing inference cost. CoAtNet captures both local and global patterns through stage-wise fusion of convolution and self-attention. We apply two ensembling strategies - greedy and uniform soup - to selectively combine diverse checkpoints into a final model. Beyond performance improvements, we analyze the ensembling effect through the lens of bias-variance decomposition. Our findings show that model soups reduces variance by stabilizing predictions across diverse model snapshots, while introducing minimal additional bias. Furthermore, using cross-entropy-based distance metrics an
  • 易漏细节梳理：

在资源有限的环境中，传统的深度学习模型往往过度拟合于虚假的相关性，导致泛化能力不足。为了解决这一问题，模型汤（Model Soup）技术应运而生，它通过平均不同检查点来稳定预测，而不会增加推理成本。CoAtNet架构能够同时捕捉局部和全局模式，而模型汤技术则通过选择几何上多样化的检查点，进一步增强了模型的多样性。与软投票相比，模型汤引入的额外偏差较小，并且能够通过使用基于交叉熵的距离度量和多维尺度（MDS）方法来选择多样化的检查点。在ICH-17数据集上，这种方法实现了最先进的性能。此外，多样性意识的检查点平均方法在数据稀缺的分类任务中显著提升了模型的泛化能力。因此，模型汤不仅能够减少预测的方差，还能够通过选择几何上多样化的检查点来增强模型的泛化能力，从而在资源有限的环境中提供更稳健的解决方案。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • conventional deep learning models in low-resource settings often overfit to spurious correlations.
  • model soups technique averages checkpoints without increasing inference cost.
  • CoAtNet architecture captures both local and global patterns.
  • greedy and uniform soup strategies selectively combine diverse checkpoints.
  • model soups reduce variance by stabilizing predictions across diverse model snapshots.
  • model soups introduce minimal additional bias compared to soft voting.
  • model soups select geometrically diverse checkpoints, unlike soft voting.
  • cross-entropy-based distance metrics and MDS show model soups selects diverse checkpoints.
  • evaluated on ICH-17 dataset, the approach achieves state-of-the-art results.
  • diversity-aware checkpoint averaging enhances generalization in data-scarce classification tasks.

[2603.02181v1] Leveraging Model Soups to Classify Intangible Cultural Heritage Images from the Mekong Delta Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2603.02181v1 (cs) [Submitted on 2 Mar 2026] Title: Leveraging Model Soups to Classify Intangible Cultural Heritage Images from the Mekong Delta Authors: Quoc-Khang Tran , Minh-Thien Nguyen , Nguyen-Khang Pham View a PDF of the paper titled Leveraging Model Soups to Classify Intangible Cultural Heritage Images from the Mekong Delta, by Quoc-Khang Tran and Minh-Thien Nguyen and Nguyen-Khang Pham View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: The classification of Intangible Cultural Heritage (ICH) images in the Mekong Delta poses unique challenges due to limited annotated data, high visual similarity among classes, and domain heterogeneity. In such low-resource settings, conventional deep learning models often suffer from high variance or overfit to spurious correlations, leading to poor generalization. To address these limitations, we propose a robust framework that integrates the hybrid CoAtNet architecture with model soups, a lightweight weight-space ensembling technique that averages checkpoints from a single training trajectory without increasing inference cost. CoAtNet captures both local and global patterns through stage-wise fusion of convolution and self-attention. We apply two ensembling strategies - greedy and uniform soup - to selectively combine diverse checkpoints into a final model. Beyond performance improvements, we analyze the ensembling effect through the lens of bias-variance decomposition. Our findings show that model soups reduces variance by stabilizing predictions across diverse model snapshots, while introducing minimal additional bias. Furthermore, using cross-entropy-based distance metrics and Multidimensional Scaling (MDS), we show that model soups selects geometrically diverse checkpoints, unlike Soft Voting, which blends redundant models centered in output space. Evaluated on the ICH-17 dataset (7,406 images across 17 classes), our approach achieves state-of-the-art results with 72.36% top-1 accuracy and 69.28% macro F1-score, outperforming strong baselines including ResNet-50, DenseNet-121, and ViT. These results underscore that diversity-aware checkpoint averaging provides a principled and efficient way to reduce variance and enhance generalization in culturally rich, data-scarce classification tasks. 49. MetaCVR: Conversion Rate Prediction via Meta Learning in Small-Scale Recommendation Scenarios

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2112.13753v5
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Different from large-scale platforms such as Taobao and Amazon, CVR modeling in small-scale recommendation scenarios is more challenging due to the severe Data Distribution Fluctuation (DDF) issue. DDF prevents existing CVR models from being effective since 1) several months of data are needed to train CVR models sufficiently in small scenarios, leading to considerable distribution discrepancy between training and online serving; and 2) e-commerce promotions have significant impacts on small scenarios, leading to distribution uncertainty of the upcoming time period. In this work, we propose a novel CVR method named MetaCVR from a perspective of meta learning to address the DDF issue. Firstly, a base CVR model which consists of a Feature Representation Network (FRN) and output layers is designed and trained sufficiently with samples across months. Then we treat time periods with different data distributions as different occasions and obtain positive and negative prototypes for each occasion using the corresponding samples and the pre-trained FRN. Subsequently, a Distance Metric Network (DMN) is devised to calculate the distance metrics between each sample and all prototypes to facil
  • 易漏细节梳理：

几个月的数据差异导致训练和在线服务之间的分布不匹配，这种不匹配增加了未来时期的分布不确定性，尤其是在电子商务促销对小规模场景有显著影响的情况下。为了解决这一问题，MetaCVR方法通过元学习处理数据分布波动问题，首先，Feature Representation Network (FRN)需要跨月样本进行充分训练，以确保其能够准确地捕捉长期趋势。其次，Distance Metric Network (DMN)计算每个样本与所有原型的距离，最近时间周期的样本用于训练DMN和Ensemble Prediction Network (EPN)，以缓解分布差异。因此，MetaCVR成为首个针对小规模推荐场景中数据分布波动问题的CVR预测研究，通过综合FRN和DMN的输出进行最终预测，从而提高模型的适应性和准确性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 几个月的数据差异导致训练和在线服务之间的分布不匹配。
  • 电子商务促销对小规模场景有显著影响，增加了未来时期的分布不确定性。
  • MetaCVR方法通过元学习处理数据分布波动问题。
  • Feature Representation Network (FRN)需要跨月样本进行充分训练。
  • Distance Metric Network (DMN)计算每个样本与所有原型的距离。
  • Ensemble Prediction Network (EPN)结合FRN和DMN输出进行最终预测。
  • 最近时间周期的样本用于训练DMN和EPN，以缓解分布差异。
  • MetaCVR是首个针对小规模推荐场景中数据分布波动问题的CVR预测研究。
正文（点击展开）

正文（抓取，非 AI）

[2112.13753v5] MetaCVR: Conversion Rate Prediction via Meta Learning in Small-Scale Recommendation Scenarios Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2112.13753v5 (cs) [Submitted on 27 Dec 2021 ( v1 ), last revised 28 Apr 2022 (this version, v5)] Title: MetaCVR: Conversion Rate Prediction via Meta Learning in Small-Scale Recommendation Scenarios Authors: Xiaofeng Pan , Ming Li , Jing Zhang , Keren Yu , Luping Wang , Hong Wen , Chengjun Mao , Bo Cao View a PDF of the paper titled MetaCVR: Conversion Rate Prediction via Meta Learning in Small-Scale Recommendation Scenarios, by Xiaofeng Pan and 6 other authors View PDF Abstract: Different from large-scale platforms such as Taobao and Amazon, CVR modeling in small-scale recommendation scenarios is more challenging due to the severe Data Distribution Fluctuation (DDF) issue. DDF prevents existing CVR models from being effective since 1) several months of data are needed to train CVR models sufficiently in small scenarios, leading to considerable distribution discrepancy between training and online serving; and 2) e-commerce promotions have significant impacts on small scenarios, leading to distribution uncertainty of the upcoming time period. In this work, we propose a novel CVR method named MetaCVR from a perspective of meta learning to address the DDF issue. Firstly, a base CVR model which consists of a Feature Representation Network (FRN) and output layers is designed and trained sufficiently with samples across months. Then we treat time periods with different data distributions as different occasions and obtain positive and negative prototypes for each occasion using the corresponding samples and the pre-trained FRN. Subsequently, a Distance Metric Network (DMN) is devised to calculate the distance metrics between each sample and all prototypes to facilitate mitigating the distribution uncertainty. At last, we develop an Ensemble Prediction Network (EPN) which incorporates the output of FRN and DMN to make the final CVR prediction. In this stage, we freeze the FRN and train the DMN and EPN with samples from recent time period, therefore effectively easing the distribution discrepancy. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first study of CVR prediction targeting the DDF issue in small-scale recommendation scenarios. Experimental results on real-world datasets validate the superiority of our MetaCVR and online A/B test also shows our model achieves impressive gains of 11.92% on PCVR and 8.64% on GMV.
